68a1(phal chen): gtor// sangs rgyas 'od kyis sprin kyang rab tu snang // sa rnams kun brgyan shing gi dam pa'i drung // kun nas nor bu'i rgyal pos rgyan byas las// bsod nams 'od kyi dbyangs kyi
68a2(phal chen): 'brug sgra 'azung // sangs rgyas rdzu 'phrul tshul yang rab tu brjod// rin chen mang po sgron ma'i char phab cing // rin chen mdzes par bkod pa rnam par mdzes// sgra dbyangs kun gyi 'brug sgra shin tu sgrog/ sa'i lnga
68a3(phal chen): rnams sa yang yang dag ston// rin chen 'od 'bro sgron ma rnam par snang // 'od zer sprin ni sa las rab tu byung // nor bu drab sil ma kun nas bkram// rin chen sna tshogs rigs kyis yan lag brgyan// sa rnams
68a4(phal chen): kun nas mdzes pa 'di dag ltos// rin chen mang po chen bzang baHna du bkye// 'gro ba dag la chos kyi rgya mtsho sgrog/ de dag chos zhing rnam par dag pa mthong // ma lus phyogs na sangs rgyas
68a5(phal chen): thams cad kyi// byang chub shing gi phun sum tshogs pa dag/ sa'i dkyil 'khor 'di na kun sdang ste// de dag chos nyid rnam par dag pa brjod// sangs rgyas gangan las chos rnams
68a6(phal chen): rgya mtsho yi// chos sgo bde bar gshegs pas gang gsungs pa// sems can kun gyi bsam pa ji bzhin du// sa 'khor rnams kyang kun nas rab tu 'byung // dri zhim 'ong rnams rtag tu 'byung bas na/ 
68a7(phal chen): de dag ji bzhin snod kyi 'gro la 'gengs// srog chags rnams kyi nyon mongs zhi bar byed// sa 'khor de nas de 'dra rab tu sgrog/ sangs rgyas rdzu 'phrul phun sum gang dag dang // dri mangs ni gang gis mdzes
68a8(phal chen): gyur pa'i// phun sum tshogs pa'i rgyan rnams re re zhing // bskal pa bye ba dag tu'ang brjod mi nus// de nas byang chub sems dpa' ye shes chen po'i sems rab tu gnon pa'i blo gros kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi
68b1(phal chen): mthus 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor yod pa thams cad la rnam par bltas te/ de'i 'tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smra so// 'jig rten kun gyi bsam pa tshim mdzad cing // sangs rgyas chos kyi gzhal yang khang ra mdzes
68b2(phal chen): 'bam klas phyogs rnams kun tu mngon sum du// sangs rgyas 'gro gsogazhal med khang na snang // rin chen kun gyis snying po rab tu brgyad// rgyan rnams kun gyis de bzhin mdzes shing 'bar// sangs
68b3(phal chen): rgyas po drang 'od ri bsam mi khab// den bzhugs shing sangs rgyas rab tu mdzes// ka ba'i rgyan ni nor bu sna tshogs te// phyogs rnams kun sgor rta babs sprin kyang bres// sngags bu'i phreng ba kun nas rgyan du
68b4(phal chen): bkong // gsar gyi dril bu'i sprin kyang rnam par brgyus// me tog bla re rnam pa sna tshogs ltos// ri rer shing sdong dar gyi bla re bras// nor bu thams cad sgo nas phreng ba 'bul// der ya
68b5(phal chen): rgya mtsho rab tu mdzes// spos dri rgyal ma tshan rin chen drang ste/ 'od zer sgron ma'i sprin gyis kun tu yog/ rgyan rnams sna rag sa kur nas shin tu bres// de na sangs rgyas rab tu 'phags
68b6(phal chen): pa bzhugs// phyogs rnams kun sgo sbal pa'i sprin gyi rnams// dbangs kyis 'jig rten khyab par grags byed cing // 'bam klas phyogs kyi sems can rnams 'dul ba// sangs rgyas po brang 'dir
68b7(phal chen): rag grag/ mdog shing dang rin nged srungs spel ba// 'phags par phyogs rnams kun tu mngon par mdzes// de la dus gsum zhing rnams thams cad kyang // gzugs brlan gyur par de dag rab tu snang / 
68b8(phal chen): phyogs rnams kun tu rin chen mang bkyib// de dag sna tshogs mdzes par rnam par 'bar/ phyogs rnams kun tu skar khung mdzes par brgyad// na babs mnga' yab sna tshogs mang pos brgyar// de
69a1(phal chen): dri meng 'ong zer kun nas snang ba yi// sangs rgyas po drang rnam pa bsal yas te// gnal med 'ang yang thams cad de la sdang // de dag kun ra'ang rgyal ba bzhugs shing mdzes/ 
69a2(phal chen): phyogs rnams kurar 'khor rnams ji snang ba// rgyal ba'i pho brang 'dir ni kun zhugs kyang // mtha' dang dpung meng lu'ang de bzhin yang // rang byung sangs rgyas po brang nger bzhugs// de nas bang chubs pas
69a3(phal chen): dpa' yon tan rin po khabasal gyis mi khyab pa ye shes rgya mtsho'i dpal gyis// sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khar rgya mtsho yod pa de dag thams cad la rnam par bltas te/ de 'i ri gsu bcad
69a4(phal chen): 'di dag smraso// sangs rgyas zhing rdul shin tu phra srid kyi// bas ngarnams rgya mtsho rnam par rab sbyangs te// sangs rgyas rdzu 'phrul smon lam yang dgazung // snying po bang chub dri meng rnam par
69a5(phal chen): mdzes// spos nim thams cad na nas yang dag rgyu// yid pa/ nanor mcheg rgyal pos kun nas brgyan// rdo rje be ma'i nar bu rgyal pos bris// shing sdeng na bor de de kur las bas/ 
69a6(phal chen): rdo rje phye ma'i nor bu 'khor lo 'thung // lhun rnams thams cad rin chen rgyan gyis brgyan// yal ga stug po sprin ltar kun nas 'khil// snying po bang rkub de na rgyal ba ladzes/ 
69a7(phal chen): yal ga dog pa kun nas mngon pa ste// 'khor rnams snur 'jam legs rnams kun tu 'phags/ me tog 'bras bu rgyun rnams kun kyang 'gyeng // snying po byang chub rgya che bas la mi khab// 'od rnams
69a8(phal chen): kye ba pogasu rnam par mdzes// dri ma med pa'i 'od 'bar zad mi shes// yal ga'i sgo nas sprin kun char yang 'bebs// snying po bang chub smon lam yangs pas byung // me tog ner dang rin cher mi zad nor// 
69b1(phal chen): ru rig ror ngag phyogs dang phyogs rnams kun nas brgyus// pe ma nor gyi gnas kyi sprin 'gyed de// sring po byang chub phyogs rnams kun tu 'byin// bde gshegs snying po byang chub 'di la ltos// pad mo'i dra 'anor bu
69b2(phal chen): dri meng mang // rin chen 'od zer dkyil 'khor kun nas 'phro// dril bu'i dra ba'i sprin gyi sgra dubangs 'byin// phyogs bcu'i shing bzang gzugs rnams gang yod pa// 'bral klas ning gi ma lus thams cad
69b3(phal chen): dag/ byang chub shing la de dag kun nas snang // de drung sangs rgyas dri med rnam par mdzes// yal ga kun nas rin chen mi zad nor// bang chub sems dpa' dag kyang stag 'thung zhing // bsod nams rgya chen dkyi
69b4(phal chen): 'khe ngabasdu/ phyogs bcur rgyal ba mchod pa de dag 'dze / de bzhin gshegs pa sngan chad cir gyur dang // byang chub skyed las byung ba'i dag smos// yal ga kun las rin chen nor
69b5(phal chen): zang sangs rgyas yul kun bsam gyis pi khab bo// de ras bang chub sems dpa' mig brgya pa pad+mo sna tshogs kyi gtsug bud kyis// sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ 'khor rgya me yod pa
69b6(phal chen): thams cad la rnal bar bltas nas/ de'i mtshogasu bsad pa 'di dag smras// dus gsum gshegs pa'i rgyal ba'i rnam 'phrul ba// de dag rin chen sgo nas kun kyang grag/ de ni mtha' dang dpung yang med pa
69b7(phal chen): sde/ sring po 'ang rab 'di la kun snang ngo // me tog mang po'i phreng ba sbyangs bkye zhing // 'od zer sprin gyis phyogs rnams kun bkang ste// byang chub shing la gnas pa'i lha tshogs rnams// sangs
69b8(phal chen): lta zhing rtag tu mtshad pa bang // spos kyi rgyal mtshan nor bu sna tshogs 'bar// spos kyi 'od 'phro bdug spos rtag tu 'byung // 'khor gyi rgya mtsho kun la khab par zhim// shing gi rgyal po dpir phyogasu
70a1(phal chen): mdzes// pad+mo 'phrul bsdug cing gser mdog 'dra// rgyal ba'i sprin sgra rtag par rab tu 'gyed// phyogs bcu'i ning rnams ma lus khab pas shing // sems can rnams kyi
70a2(phal chen): nyon mongs gdung ba sal// rgyal ba'i 'khor ni tshad mang rgya che ste// phyogs rnams kun nas snying po byang chub la// gzugs brlan snang zhing dri med 'ong mchog 'gyeng // byang chub shing gi rnam 'phrul 'di dag ltos
70a3(phal chen): smon lam sgra dang dbyangs kyi mar me rnams// rin chen sna tshogs yal ga kun las 'bar// srid pa rgya mtsho kun na sngan chad du// rgyal ba'i spyod pa ji ltar byung ba ston// bang rub lha rnams zhing gi rdul sred
70a4(phal chen): de dag thams cad snying po byang chub gnas/ thub pa'i byang chub shing la skad cig cing // rnam thar gzhan dang gzhan mang de dag ston// rang byung spyad pa thams cad spyod pa'i tshe// sngan
70a5(phal chen): cha nga bzhin gshegs pa gang mchod pa// de dag mtshan bcas sngon gyi sbyor bcas pa// thams cad rin chen sgo nas rab tu snang // phyogs bcu'i sems can ji srid sdeng gyur pa/ 
70a6(phal chen): dag thams cad 'di las sgra 'byung ste// de dag cis 'dul rnam dag ci 'dra ba'ang // snying po byang chub 'di las kun brjod do// byang chub shing rnams mtha' yas phyogs kun na// bsam gyis mi khyab rgyan gyi
70a7(phal chen): sprin can dag/ mtha' yas sna tshogs rgyan can thams cad kyang // sngan chad de bzhin gshegs pas yongs sbyangs pa'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' gser gyi 'od 'phro gzi brjid dkyil 'khor gyi 'od
70a8(phal chen): kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor yod pa thams cad la rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smras// srid pa'i rgya mtsho ra byang chub spyod mdzad che// mos pa'i
70b1(phal chen): dkyil 'khor yongasu smon dag cing // gnas dang gnas min stobs rnams thugs chung ba'i// bder gshegs sa stobs rnam par dag pa mthong // bskal pa kun du rgya mtsho las sbyangs te// masam nyid chos
70b2(phal chen): bsgoms ji ltar bsgrubs pa'i rnams// sangs rgyas 'od las de bzhin phyogs bkang zhing // las rnams rgya mtsho de bzhin rab tu brjod// sna tshogs thabs kyis 'bam klas stobs skyong che// bskal pa snga
70b3(phal chen): mar 'gro ba'i dbang po bzhin// yongasu smin pas de bas 'khor kun kyang // sems dag sangs rgyas dbang po'i stobs la 'jug/ 'jig rten kun gyi mos pa sna tshogs dang // bsam pa ji bzhin sbyor ba rnam
70b4(phal chen): spyod pa// de dag ji bzhin rgyal ba chos ston te// rang byung mos pa mkhyen pa'i stobs ston to// phyogs rnams ma lus zhing rnams rgya mtsho dang // 'bum klas sems cad khams pa
70b5(phal chen): chos kyi khams// na mkha'i khams rnams mnyam nyid mkhyen mi rtog/ rang byung spu rtser khams mkhyen stobs kyang ston// bder gshegs ye shes rgya chen kun tu 'gro/ skad cig
70b6(phal chen): gcig gis dus gsum ma lus 'gengs// phyogs dang zhing dang bskal pa 'gro bkang zhing // sems can kun la stobs 'jug mngon par bstan// bsam gtan rnam thar stobs sa mtha' dpung med// 
70b7(phal chen): ting 'dzin rgya mtsho'i tshul ni 'gro kun snang // thams cad rgyal ba'i sku la bstan pas na// sems can bsam pa'i gnas kyi non mongs sal// sangs rgyas ye shes dus gsum bsgribs pa med/ 
70b8(phal chen): skad cig kun la dus gsum spu rtser ston// zhing dang sems can sangs rgyas de bzhin chos// de ltar rgyal bas rjesu dran stobs bstan// thub pa'i spyan ni na mkha' ma'am pa ste// des ni chos dbyings ma
71a1(phal chen): lus gsal bar gzigs// thams cad tshul gyis chags med gzhal yas sa// brnyas pas ye shes spyan ni rnam mang bstan// 'jig rten kun gyi sbyor mang ji skad
71a2(phal chen): dang // 'gro ba'i bag chags bgazhal ma lus par// thabs sgo kun nas nyon mongs zhi mdzad cing // rgyal ba 'jig rten gang bar kun nas byung // de nas byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi dbyings kun nas
71a3(phal chen): sgrog pas// sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ 'khor rgya mtsho yod pa thams cad la rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smras// rgya chen sangs rgyas byin rlabs phyogs kun tu// sangs rgyas
71a4(phal chen): sngon kyang rtog pa mi mnga' ste// pha rol phyin pa rgya chen yongs bkang ba// byang chub spyod pa rgya chen de dag snang // 'gro ba rnams la thugs rje che bskyed cing // sbyin pa'i mthar pir sngan
71a5(phal chen): chang spyad pas na// de phyir thub pa'i sku ni mtshan gyis rgyan// 'gro ba kun gyis blta zhing dga' ba skye// bskal pa rgya ma tshe mang po mtha' yas sngon// tshul khrims pha rol phyin pa
71a6(phal chen): yongs sbyangs pas// daphyir bskal pa phyogasu dri med cing // shin tu 'phags par 'jig rten sdug bsngal sel// ma log mnyam pa nyid la dang bskyed de// sngan chad bzod pa'i dkyil 'khor rnam sbyangs
71a7(phal chen): pas// 'gro dang mtshungs mnyam yon tan kun ston te// de bas phyog su 'od rnams shin tu 'phro// bskal pa rgya mtsho mang por sngon spyod tshe// 'gro ba rnams kyi bsgribs pa thibs po bstsal// de
71a8(phal chen): phyir pogs bcu'i 'gro ba kun bkang ste// shing rab drung na rgyal ba mngon par mdzes// bsam gtan yan lag rgya mtsho sbyong ba'i tshe// bskal pa yangs par rgyal bas rab tu spyad// de bas 'gro
71b1(phal chen): ba'i gnal med dga' bskyed// 'on mongs dri ma bsgring ba kun kyang sel// sangs rgyas rgya mtsho'i drung du sngon spyod cing // shes rab mthar phyin rgyal bas sngon bkang ste/ 'gro ba'i gti mug mun pa yong
71b2(phal chen): su bsal// de bas rgyal ba kun tu rnam par mdzes// 'gro ba kun mas ma thabs sgo thams cad kyis// yang dag zung zhing 'gro ba rnam sbyangs pas// phyogs rnams kur kun la mngon par bzhugs/ 
71b3(phal chen): pi ma'i bskal par 'gro ba mngon du lta// smon lam pha rol phyin pa rab sbyong che// bskal pa rgya mtsho shin tu rgya che zhing // phyi mtha'i bskal par 'gro ba'i sprin mnyam par// spyad pas de par 'gro ba kur
71b4(phal chen): mdzes// rgyal bas chos kun stobs kyi mthar phyin pa// skol ba gnal yas mang por yongs sbyangs// de phyir rang byung stobs kyi pha rol phyin// phyogs kyi zhing rnams kun na pa
71b5(phal chen): 'phags// thams cad mkhyen zhing namakha' mtshungs man/ ma bi'i// ye shes kun gyi sgo nas sngon sbyangs pas/ dpyir chags med ye shes po rol phyin// phyogs bcu kun
71b6(phal chen): rargyal ba mngon par mdzes// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sprin yid du 'ong ba dri ma med pa'i zla bas// sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ 'khor rgya mtsho yod pa thams cad la rnam par bltas nas/ de
71b7(phal chen): tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smras// sangs rgyas rdzu 'phrul yul ni phyogs rnams kyi// 'gro ba'i rgyud dbyings na mkha' mnyam par snang // sa rnams yangs pa ji ltar sngon bskyed pa// de bzhin kun
71b8(phal chen): kyang rin chen sgo nas brjod// dang po'i sa ni dga' ba'i shugs kyi yul// phyogs dbyings kun gyi bder gshegs rnams mthong zhing // gzhal med bskal par dri med yongs sbyangs pas// chos
72a1(phal chen): dbyings yangs la ye shes rab tu byung // thams cad chos la dri mengs gnyis te// bskal pa rgya mtsho mang por rnam spyad cing // rgyal ba tshad med rgya mtsho mchod pas nas/ 
72a2(phal chen): 'gro ba tshad med dri med sbyangs pas byung // bsod nams dkyil 'khor 'od ni sa gsum ste// snying po bzod pa'i dkyil 'khor lhag mthong brtan// gang du de skyes rin chen sgo dag nas// chos kyi
72a3(phal chen): sprin ni rgya chen rab tu thos/ 'od 'phro rgya mtsho ldan pa gzhal med sa// mthu'i 'khor 'od snying po snying rje ste// zhing rnams kun tu sgrib dang mnyam pi'i lus// 'gro ba'i son mongs kun nas rnam sbya
72a4(phal chen): pa'o// dka' rgyal snying po mnyam dbyings mnyam zhing de// zhing rnams kun tu 'gro zhing zhi la gzhol// sangs rgyas chos yul kun nas rab tu skyes// de yang rnam dag ji bzhin rgyal bas bstan
72a5(phal chen): shes rab rgya mtsho yangs pa'i sprin la spyod// 'bum klas tshe sa kyi mthar thug rnam pa kun// zhing rnams kun la ma na sum na mkha' 'dra// de 'thung byang chub shing chen 'di las grag
72a6(phal chen): chos dbyings mkha' dang 'dra ba'i lus can te// 'gro ba kun 'gengs 'gro ba kun snang byed// 'byam klas thabs kyi sgo nas rnam par dag/ ring du song mchog de ni rgyal bas bstan// thams cad chos dang
72a7(phal chen): smon lam spyod mang dang // zhing rnams rgya mtsho'i dbyings kyang mnyam rtogs pas// bskal pa kun tu 'gro mchog mi g.yo ste// gzhal med sa de'i sprin kyang rab tu sgrog/ tshad med yul can stobs
72a8(phal chen): kyis rab tu snang // rdzu 'phrul stobs kyis 'gro zhing stobs la 'jug/ 'di ni rdul med dge ba'i blo gros sa// bskal pa rgya mtshor byang chub shing las brjod// chos kyi sprin ni rgya chen sa bcu ste/ 
72b1(phal chen): dus rnams kun 'gengs na mkha'i rang bzhin 'dra// sangs rgyas yul gyi sgra dang dbyangs kun tu// rgyal ba'i byin gyis 'di las rab tu grag/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' rnam par gnon pa gti mug med pa'i
72b2(phal chen): 'od zer gyi rgyal mtshan gyis// sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ phyogs bcur rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smoso// rnam pa du mar 'khor rnams gnas pa ni// dad pa sna tshogs
72b3(phal chen): yongasu dag pa'i sems// rgyan dang yul rnams kun la rab tu zhugs// de dag sangs rgyas ye shes 'jug par 'gyur// phan tshun smon lam rnam dag spyod yul te/ 
72b4(phal chen): dag pa mtha' yas bya ba rab tu byas// de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam 'phrul thams cad kyang // gzhan dang gzhan gyi sgo nas rab tu mthong // bdar gshegs chos kyi sku la zhugs pa dag
72b5(phal chen): la las rgyal ba'i chos sku de nyid la// kun tu sprin 'dra gzhal med chags med pa'i// mtha' yas chos kyi rang bzhin chos nyid mthong // la las rgyal ba'i gzugs sku de zhing la/ 
72b6(phal chen): phyogs bcu kun tu rnam par 'phrul mdzad cing // yon tan mtha' yas 'od sbyin rab 'bar ba// 'gro ba dang tshul sprin du gyur par mthong // la la rgyal ba'i ye shes chags med 'jug/ dus gsum man
72b7(phal chen): zhing mkha' dang 'dra ba'i sku// 'gro ba kun gyi bsam pa'i tshul 'byung ba'i// sangs rgyas stobs la rab tu 'jug par mthong // sangs rgyas gsung ni thogs pa med 'byung ste// phyogs kun zhing
72b8(phal chen): rnams ma lus rgyas 'gyur zhing // 'gro ba snod bzhin skul bar byed pa yi// de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung la la la 'jug/ la la sangs rgyas snang ba sna tshogs 'jug/ sna tshogs snang bas 'gro ba
73a1(phal chen): kun bkang zhing // rgyal ba'i rdzu 'phrul kun tu snang mdzad pa'i// sangs rgyas 'ang ni la las der yang mthong // baspu'i sgo nas 'od zer rab bkye ba'i// 'od zer rgya mcho
73a2(phal chen): sprin la la la 'jug/ sngan chad rgyal ba'i spyod pa bstan pa la// la la dga' zhing rgyal ba shes par byed// la las bsod nams sna tshogs mtshan gyi rnams// bder gshegs bsod nams byung ba
73a3(phal chen): ji bzhin mthong // pha rol phyin pa rgya mtsho sbyong ba'i tshe// ji ltar ngag gyur mtshan kyang la las mthong // sgo rnams kun nas rgyal ba tshad med de// mtha' dang dpung med chos kyi dbyings bkang zhing
73a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas byin rlabs rab tu brjod pa kun// rnam 'a phrul sangs rgyas yul ni la las mthong // de nas sangs rgyas kyis byin gyis brlabs kyis// 'jig rten gyi khams
73a5(phal chen): me tog gi rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i gzhi dang snying po rgya mtsho tham sa cad rnam pa drug tu g.yos so// rab tu g.yos/ kun tu g.yos// 'gul to// rab tu 'gul te/ ku tu
73a6(phal chen): 'gul to// ldeg go/ rab tu ldeg go// kun tu ldego/ che mchem/ rab tu chem chem/ kun tu chem che mo// 'ur rur/ rab tu 'ur 'ur/ kun tu 'ur 'ur ro// shig shig/ 
73a7(phal chen): rab tu shig shig/ kun tu shig shig go// 'jig rten gyi dbang po de dag thams cad re res kyang mchod pa mngon par sgrub pa'i sprin bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i char de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor
73a8(phal chen): du mngon par rab tu phab bo// 'di ltar spos kyi me tog sna tshogs kyi char thams cad rab tu phab bo// rin po che sna tshogs thams cad kyi sprin dang rin po che'i 'od 'phro ba'i pang po'i dra ba thams
73b1(phal chen): cad kyi sprin dang / ner bu rin po che'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor kha dog mtha' yas pa'i sprin dang / rin po che kha dog sna tshogs dang / mu tig thams cad kyi sprin dang / spos dang / tsan dan rin po che thams
73b2(phal chen): cad kyi sprin dang / rin po che'i gdugs thams cad kyi sprin dang / nor bu'i rgyal po sgra dbangs bzang po yid du 'ong ba'i sprin dang / nor bu nyi ma'i 'od zer gyi phreng ba mang po'i sprin dang / rin po che'i
73b3(phal chen): 'od zer gyi mdzod thams cad kyi sprin dang / rang rang gi lus las rgyan thams cad 'byung ba'i sprin dang / de lta bu dag la sogs pa 'jig rten gyi dbang po res kyang mchod pa mngon par sgrub pa'i sprin
73b4(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i/ char de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho thams cad du mngon par phab bo// ji ltar 'jig rten gyi khams 'dir 'jig rten gyi dbang
73b5(phal chen): rnams rab tu dga' bar gyur pa de bzhin du gzhi dang snying po ma tog gi rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgya ma'i 'jig rten gyi dbang por res kyang mchod pa mngon par spru
73b6(phal chen): de'i sprin gyi char de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho dag tu rab tu phab par gyur to// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na yang 'jig rten gyi dbang po rnams mos pa ga' rang
73b7(phal chen): dmigs pa gzhan dang gzhan/ ting 'dzir gyi tshul gyi sgo rgya mtsho gzhan dang gzhan dang / tshogs gzhan dang gzhan dang / yang dag par sgrub pa gzhan dang gzhan dang / dga' shugs kyis spyod pa

74a1(phal chen): gzhan dang / yul dang stobs la 'jug pa gzhan dang gzhan dang / rnam par thar pa'i tshul rgya mtsho'i sgo gzhan dang gzhan dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po byang chub

74a5(phal chen): rgyas kyis ni ji lta bu zhig mngar/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams la sangs rgyas kyi yul ni ji lta bu zhig ma ngar/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams la byin gyis

74b7(phal chen): lnga bu zhig tu yongasu ston// byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la rab tu 'jug pa rgya mtsho thams cad ni ji lta bu zhig tu yongasu ston/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la tshogs rgya mtsho thams cad

75a1(phal chen): ni ji lta bu zhig du yongs su ston/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la spyod pa rgya mtsho rnams ni ji lta bu zhig du yongasu sngon/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la 'a

75a5(phal chen): rnams kyi bsapa pa ji lta ba bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams rgya ma tsho rnams kyang bstan pa mdzad grang / sems can rgya mtsho rnam sa kyang bstan pa mdzad grang / sangs rgyas rgya mtsho rnams kyang

75b5(phal chen): gsal// de ba'i gshegs pa'i spyod yul ci yis 'jugargyal ba'i mkhyen li ji ltar 'jug pa dang // rgya chen mtha'ayas stobs rnams rnam sbyang ba// rgyal sras kun la yang dag

75b7(phal chen): gsol// ji ltar chos rgyal po brang mngar mdzad cing // rgyal ba'i spyod yul ji ltar mi 'phrogs dang // sangs rgyas ches gzhar rgya chen de dag kyang // thugs brtse'i sang du yang dag bsngar tu gas pa
75b8(phal chen): rgyal ba'i spyan ni ji ltar tshang mang 'ang // skar dang shangs dang de bzhir ljags dang sku// sangs rgyas thugs kyang ji ltar mtha' yas pa// 'di dag tshul la 'jug pa bstan tu gsol// zhing rnams rgya ma
76a1(phal chen): ltar sems can khams// chos dbyings tshul rnams rgya mtsho de dag dang // sangs rgyas rgya mtsho mtha' dang dpung med pa// 'di dag rgyal ba'i sras la bstan du gsol/

79a5(phal chen): brlabs pa dang / rin po che thams cad kyi me tog gi ze ba'i khang pa brtsegs pa'i sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog pa rwa bin gyis brlabs pa dang / rin po che'i phreng bas yongasu brgyan
79a6(phal chen): pa'i khang pa brtsegs pa'i sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / 'od zer gyi snang ba phyogs kun tu 'phro ba'i snying po dang ldan pa'i khang pa brtsegs pargyan thams cad 'byung
79a7(phal chen): ba'i sprin banus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / rin po che'i tshon thams cad kyis rab tu brgyan cing rgyan du ma yang dag par ston pa'i khang pa brtsegs pa'i sprin bcus na mkha'
79a8(phal chen): kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / phyogs thams cad kyis rab tu brgyan par kun tu rgyas par 'gengs pa'i khang pa brtsegs pa'i sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs
79b1(phal chen): pa dang / ske kun tu me tog gi rta babs dang / dril bu'i dra ba bres pa'i khang pa brtsegs pa'i sprin bcus namakha' kun nas yog par bir gyis brlabs pa dang / de dag la sogs pa khang pa brtsegs pa'i sprir 'jig
79b2(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs par byed cing / bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der phyin te/ bcom ldan 'das la lag 'tshal nas/ nub
79b3(phal chen): phyogs su brten te seng ge'i khri rin po che'i pangad mo chen po lo ma sna tshogs gser las byas pa'i snying po can mngon par sprul nas skyil mo dkrung bcas te/ 'khod par gyur to// de nas yang 'jig rten gyi khams
79b4(phal chen): rgya mtsho 'di dang / mdang chags byung phyogs na 'jig rten gyi kha mas rgya mtsho bai DUR+Sha pad+mo'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sring po zhes bya ba yod de/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud de dag las 'jig
79b5(phal chen): na gyi khams me tog ud pa li'i rgyanan/ de bzhin gsheg sa pa ye shes kyi dpal kun tu dbyangs kyi rgyal po bzhug sa pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho nas/ byang chu
79b6(phal chen): sems dpa' seng ge'i 'od zer snang bas mthu 'byin pa'i blo gros shes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang lhan cig tu 'phags nas/ bcom ldan
79b7(phal chen): 'das gang na ba der 'ong bar gyur te/ spos dang / nor bu sna tshogs thams cad kyi shing gi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis rlob cing / sgro thams cad nas lo ma'i dog pa'i srin 'thung
79b8(phal chen): ba'i spos shing gi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / shing gi gzugs thams cad las rgyan mtha' yas pa yongasu ston pa'i shing gi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog
80a1(phal chen): padu'i gyis byas pa dang / me cho ga thams cad kyi sbyin rabatun pa'i matog gi shing gi sprin banus rnamakha' kun nas log pa byin gyis brlabs pa dang / rin po'i
80a2(phal chen): ba'i dkyil 'khor thams cad kyis rnam par snang bar bas pa'i shing gi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / tsan dan gyi pha ma thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lus par yang
80a3(phal chen): dag par ston pa'i shing gi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / sngon gyi snying po byang chub kyi rgyan bsam gyis mi khyab pa rab tu ston pa'i shing ga smer bsus namakha' kun nas sos
80a4(phal chen): par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / kha dog mtha' yas pa'i gos kyi mdzod kyi nyi mas rnam par snang ba byas pa'i shing gi sbyin pa nus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / sgra
80a5(phal chen): dbyangs thams cad rab tu sgrog cing yid du 'ong ba'i sgra kun tu ga tong ba'i shing gi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / de dag la sogs pa shing gi sprin 'jig
80a6(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba skad kyis na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs par byed cing / bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der yin te/ bcom ldan 'das la phag 'tshal nas/ bang
80a7(phal chen): phyogasu brten te/ seng ge'i khri nor bu sgron ma'i pad+mo'i snying po can mngon par sprul nas/ dkyil mo dkrung bcas te 'khong par gyur to// de nas 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'di dang / mdab chagasu
80a8(phal chen): bang dang / shar gyi phyogs mtshams na 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'dzam bu chu klung dang / shel gyi kha dog tshon gyi rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba yod de/ 'jig rten gyi khams bar ma'i rgyud de dag las
80b1(phal chen): 'jig rter gyi khams rin po che'i rgyan sna tshogs kyi snying po na/ de bzhin gshegs pa chos thams cad la mi 'jigs pa'i sgron ma bzhugs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho nas byang chub sems dpa' chos
80b2(phal chen): kyi yon tan gyi mdzod mi zad pa'i dpal gyi gzi brjid mar me zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang lhan cig tu 'phags nas/ bcom ldan 'das gang na ba
80b3(phal chen): der 'ong bar gyur te/ seng ge'i khri rin po che kha dog mtha' yas pa'i pad mo'i sring po can gyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par bin gyis rlob cing / seng ge'i khri nor bu'i rgyal po kun tu mngon pas rnam par
80b4(phal chen): snang bar bas pa'i snying po can gyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yo ga par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / seng ge'i khri rgyan mang po thams cad kyis rab tu brgyan pa'i snying po can gyi sprin bcus
80b5(phal chen): dmakha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / seng ga'i khri rin po che 'od 'phro ba'i sgron ma sna tshogs kyi phreng ba'i snying po can gyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par 'i
80b6(phal chen): sa brlabs pa dang / seng ge'i khri phyogs kun nas phreng ba rin po che'i char 'bebs pa'i snying po can gyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / seng ge'i khri spos kyi re
80b7(phal chen): 'ad+mo'i phreng ba rin po che thams cad kyi sring po can gyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas log par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / seng ge re khri sangs rgyas kyi gdan thams cad kyi rgyan yang dag par ston pa'i nor ba
80b8(phal chen): rgyal po'i sring po can gyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / seng ge'i khri rgyan dang phreng ba thams cad 'phang zhing rta babs dang stegs bus rab tu brgyan pa'i snying po can gyi sprin bcus
81a1(phal chen): na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / seng ge'i khri shing thams cad kyi yal ga las nor bu rin po che dang phye ma 'byung ba'i snying po can gyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas
81a2(phal chen): yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / seng ge'i khri spos dang rin po che'i tshogs kyis kun nas brgyan pa'i nyi mas rnam par snang bar byas pa'i snying po can gyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs
81a3(phal chen): pa dang / de dag la sogs pa seng ga'i khri'i sprin 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs par byed cing / bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der yin te/ 
81a4(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das la phag 'tshal nas byang dang / shar gyi phyogs mtsham su brten te/ seng ge'i khri nor bu rin po che snang ba'i rgyal mtshan gyi pad mo sna tshogs kyi snying po can mngon par
81a5(phal chen): sprul nas/ skyil mo dkrung bcas te 'khod par gyur to// de nas yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'di dang / mngab chagasu shar dang lho'i phyogs mtshams na/ 'jig rten gyi khams
81a6(phal chen): rgya mtsho bai DUR+Ya'i 'od zer kun tu snang ba gser gyi rgyan ces bya ba yod de/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud de dag las 'jig rten gyi khams spos kyi dpal dri ma med par snang ba na/ de bzhin gshegs pa
81a7(phal chen): kun tu dga' ba'i shugs dpal gyi rgyal po bzhugs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho nas byang chub sems dpa' ye shes kyi 'od zer shes rab kun nas sgron mi'i blo gros shes bya ba/ byang chub
81a8(phal chen): sems dpa' 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba sbed dang lhan cig tu 'phags te/ bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der 'ong bar gyur te/ nor bu yid bzhin gyi rgyal po thams cad kyi bla re'i sprin bcus
81b1(phal chen): ram kha kun nas yog par ben gyis brlabs pa dang / rin po che in dra nI la'i ze ba can gyi me tog thams cad kyi rgyan gyi bla re'i sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang
81b2(phal chen): sdes rin po che'i bla re thams cad kyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / rin po che 'od 'phro ba sgron ma'i gzugs kyi bla re'i sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis
81b3(phal chen): brlabs pa dang / nor bu'i rgyal po sangs rgyas kyi rdzu 'phrul dang / 'od dang / sgra dbyangs rab tu ston pa'i bla re'i sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / nor bu
81b4(phal chen): dang gos dang / rgyan thams cad kyi gzugs brnyan yang dag par ston pa'i bla re'i sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / me tog thams cad kyi dog pa lnga
81b5(phal chen): bu rin po che'i bla re'i sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / dril bu sna tshogs kun tu sgras khyab par byed pa'i dra ba'i bla re'i sprin bcus na mkha
81b6(phal chen): kun ras yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / pad+mo'i dra ba mtha' yas pa sna tshogs rin po che'i snying po can gyi bla re'i sprin bcus nam mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / gas
81b7(phal chen): gyi za ba 'od 'phro zhing snang ba'i rgyal mtshan gyi bla re'i sprin banus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / rgyan bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i gzugs brnyan rab tu ston pa'i rgyan thams
81b8(phal chen): cad kyis brgyan pa'i bla ra'i sprin banus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / de dag la sogs pa bla re'i sprin 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis na mkha'
82a1(phal chen): kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs par byed cing / bcom ldan 'das gangar ba der byin nas/ bcom ldan 'das la phyag 'tshal te/ shar dang lho'i phyogs mtshams
82a2(phal chen): su brtan te/ seng ge'i khri pang mo sna tshogs rin po ches rab tu brgyan pa'i sring po can mngon par sprul nas/ skyil mo dkrung bcas te 'khong ngo // de nas yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgyam
82a3(phal chen): 'di dang / mdab chags su lho dang nub kyi phyogs mtshams na/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho zhi pa'i 'od zer rab tu 'ab bas kun tu snang ba'i snying po zhes bya ba yod de/ 'jig rten gyi khams par
82a4(phal chen): rgyud de dag las/ 'jig rten gyi khams nyi ma dang seng ge ltar sna da ban/ de bzhin gshegs pa sgo kun nas ye shes rnam bar snang ba'i dbyings bzhugs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya
82a5(phal chen): mtshonas/ byang chub sems dpa' me tog kun nas 'od bro gnug pud rab tu 'phyang ba zhes bya ba/ byang chub sem sa dpa' 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba
82a6(phal chen): snyeng dang lhan cig tu 'phags te/ bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der 'ong bar gyur te/ sna tshogs thams cad kyis brgyan pa'i rin po che'i gdugs kyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par
82a7(phal chen): byin gyis rlob cing / 'od zer snang ba'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i me tog gi gdugs kyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / mu tig mang po kha dog mtha' yas pa zam
82a8(phal chen): cad kyi gdugs kyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / nor bu'i rgyal po byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi snying rje'i sgo nas rab tu sgrog pa'i gdugs kyi sprin bcus
82b1(phal chen): namakha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / rin po che'i 'od 'phro ba sna tshogs kyi phreng ba'i gdugs kyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / rin po che'i tshon rnam pa sna tshog
82b2(phal chen): kyi 'od kyis rab tu brgyan cing dril bu'i dra ba bres pa'i gdugs kyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / rin po che'i shing gi yal ga thams cad kyis brgyan pa'i gzugs kyi sprin
82b3(phal chen): bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / nor bu'i rgyal po nyi ma rnam par snang ba'i lte ba'i gdugs kyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / spos dang bdu
82b4(phal chen): pa thams cad kyi gdugs kyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / tsan dan gyi phye ma mngo bas kun tu rgyas par 'gengs pa'i gdugs kyi sprin bcus na mkha'
82b5(phal chen): kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi yul rgya chen po rnam par bstan pas kun tu rgyun gyis khyab par byed pa'i gdugs kyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par
82b6(phal chen): byin gyis brlabs pa dang / de dag la sogs pa gdugs kyi sprin 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis nam mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs par bidi cing / bcom ldan 'das
82b7(phal chen): gang na bder pin te/ bcom ldan 'das la phag 'tshal nas/ lho dang / nub kyi phyogs mtsham su bstan te/ seng ge'i khri in dra nI la yid du 'ong bar 'bar ba'i 'od zer gyi snying po can dag mngon
82b8(phal chen): bar sprul nas skyil mo dkrung bcas te 'khong ngo // de nas yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'di dang mdab chagasu/ nub dang byang gi phyogs mtshams na/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho rin po che'i 'o
83a1(phal chen): zer 'bar ba'i skar mnga' 'od kyi snying po zhes bya ba yod de/ 'jig rten gyi khams bar ma'i rgyud de dag las 'jig rten gyi khams spos kyi rgyan yid du 'ong ba'i snying po na/ de bzhin
83a2(phal chen): gshegs pa yon tan rgya mtsho tshad med pa'i 'od bzhugs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho nas/ byang chub sems dpa' 'od zer dang / gzi brjid mi zad pa'i rgyal po'i blo gros shes bya ba/ byang chub

83a4(phal chen): gyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis rlob cing / rin po che 'od 'phro ba'i gzugs kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin pa nus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlangs pa dang / me
83a5(phal chen): tog gi sprin gyis rnam par snang bar byas pa'i 'od kyi dkyil 'kho ra gyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brla bas pa dang / 'od zer gyi sgo nas sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa'i 'od
83a6(phal chen): kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin bcus rnamakha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing gzugs rlan gyi khongasu chud pa'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin ba nas rnamakha
83a7(phal chen): kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / rin po che'i yal ga'i sgo kun nas sangs rgyas kyi yul rab tu sgrog pa'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa
83a8(phal chen): dang / nor bu'i rgyal po rin po che bai DUR+Ya'i rigs kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / sems skad cig gis sems can mtha' yas pa'i
83b1(phal chen): gzugs yongs ston pa'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin bcus namakha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi smon lam 'thung ba'i sgra yid du 'ong b.rab tu gtong ba'i 'od
83b2(phal chen): dkyil 'khor gyi sprin banus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad du sems can 'dul ba'i sgra sgrog pa/ nor bu'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin bcus
83b3(phal chen): nam mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / de dag la sogs pa 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs
83b4(phal chen): par byer cing / bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der yin te/ bcom ldan 'das la phag 'tshal nas/ nub dang bang gi phyogs ma tshams su brtan te/ seng ge'i khri 'od zer 'bar ba mi zad pa'i

83b6(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bad mo dri zhim dpal gyi snying po zhes bya ba yod de/ 'jig rten gyi khams bar ma'i rgyud de dag las 'jig rten gyi khams rin po che'i seng ge snang zhing 'bar ba dang / de bzhin
83b7(phal chen): gshegs pa chos kyi dbyings snang bar mdzad pa'i 'od zer bzhugs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho nas/ byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi dbyingasu 'od 'phro ba rnam par snang ba 'byung ba'i blo gras

84a1(phal chen): 'od zer gyi sprin bcus namakha' kun nas log par byin gyis rlob cing / spos thams cad kyi 'od zer gyi sprin bcus namakha' kun nas yog par 'byin gyis brlabs pa dang
84a2(phal chen): rin po che'i 'od 'phro ba thams cad kyi 'od zer gyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad brjod pas khyab par byed pa'i 'od zer gyi sprin bcus namakha' kun

84a4(phal chen): pa brtsegs pa thams cad kyi 'od zer gyi sprin pa nus na mkha' ku na nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / bskal pa thams cad gcig nas gcig tu brgyud par sangs rgyas yang dag par 'thung
84a5(phal chen): zhing sems can yongasu smin par bya ba brjod pa'i 'od zer gyi spyi na bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / rin po che zad mi shes pa thams cad dang / me tog thams
84a6(phal chen): cad kyi ze ba'i 'od zer gyi sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / de dag la sogs pa 'od zer gyi sprin 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis na mkha'
84a7(phal chen): kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs par byed cing / bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der phyin nas/ bcom ldan 'das la phyag 'tshal te/ 'og gi phyogs su brten nas seng ge'i khri rin po che'i sgron ma rab tu
84a8(phal chen): 'bar ba 'byung ba'i sring po can dag mngon par sprul nas skyil mo dkrung bcas te 'khod do// de nas yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mcho ga ni dang / snying po ma tog gi rgyan gyis brgyan pa'ing dang mang bachas
84b1(phal chen): su/ steng gi phyogs na 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho nor bu rin po che sna tshogs kyi rgya mtsho'i rgyan ces bya ba yod de/ 'jig rten gyi khams par mi'i rgyud de dag las 'jig rten gyi khams mtshan yid du 'ong ba
84b2(phal chen): rnam par snang ba zhes bya ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa yon tan dang grags pa thogs pa med pa'i rnam par thar pa rab tu snang ba'i rgyal po bzhugs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho nas/ byang chub sems dpa
84b3(phal chen): stobs dang / brtson 'grus chags pa med pa'i blo gros shes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang lhan cig tu 'phags nas/ bcom ldan 'das gang nab
84b4(phal chen): der 'ong bar gyur te/ rin po che kha dog mtha' yas par 'od 'phro ba'i sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlob cing / nor bu rin po che kun nas 'od kyi dra ba 'od 'phro ba'i sprin bcus
84b5(phal chen): dmakhar kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rgyan rgya chen pos rnam par snang bar 'od 'phro ba'i sprin banus na mkha' kun nas yog
84b6(phal chen): bar byin gyis brlabs pa dang / spos thams cad 'phro ba'i sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / rgyan thams cad 'od 'phro ba'i sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin
84b7(phal chen): gyis brlabs pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul 'od 'phro ba'i sprin bcus nas kha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / shing dang ze ba rnam pa sna tshog su 'od 'phro ba'i sprin bcus
84b8(phal chen): mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / rdo rje sna tshogs 'od 'phro ba'i sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / nor bu'i rgyal po byang chub sems dpa'i spyod
85a1(phal chen): mtha' yas pa brjod cing 'od 'phro ba'i sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / mu tig gi sgron ma 'od 'phro ba'i sprin bcus na mkha' kun nas yog
85a2(phal chen): par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / de dag la sogs pa 'od 'phro ba'i sprin 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis na mkha' kun nas yog par byin gyis brlabs par byed cing / bcom ldan
85a3(phal chen): 'das gang na bder phyin te/ bcom ldan 'das la phyag 'tshal nas/ steng gi phyog su brten te/ seng ge'i khri sangs rgyas kyi gsung sgrog pa'i 'od zer 'byung ba'i pad+mo'i sring po can dag mngon par
85a4(phal chen): sprul nas/ skyil mo dkrung bcas te 'khod ngo // de dag la so gas pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed nas kyang / byang chub
85a5(phal chen): sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byang chub sems dpa' re re zhing yang byang chub se mas dpa' 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba
85a6(phal chen): snyed kyis bskor cing mdun du byas te/ byang chub sems dpa' re re zhing yang rgyan rnam pa sna tshogs kyi mchod pa'i sprin 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba sred kyis na mkha' kun nas
85a7(phal chen): log par byin gyis brjeb tsong 'ongs par gyur te phyin nas gang nas 'ongs pa'i phyog suM brten te/ seng ge'i khri rin po che sna tshogs kyi rgyan gyi snying po can dag mngon par sprul cing / skyil
85a8(phal chen): dkrung bcas te 'khod par gyur to// 'khod pa'i rjes la byang chub sems dpa' de dag gi ba spu'i khung bu thams cad re re nas 'od zer gyi sprin rin po che thams cad ltar kha gi sna tshogs pa'i 'jig
85b1(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba sred rab tu byung bar gyur to// rin po che re re'i sgo nas kyang byang chub sems dpa' seng ge'i khri pad+ma'i snying po can la 'khor pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu'i rdul
85b2(phal chen): shin tu phra bsnyed rab tu byung bar gyur to// byang chub sems dpa' re res kyang chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul rgya mtsho'i khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba thams cad kyi sbubs gang brlabs nas/ rdul shin tu phra ba re ra la
85b3(phal chen): yang zhing 'bam klas pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba skad du rab tu 'jug par 'gyur to// zhing re rer yang dus gsum du gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das thams cad mthong zhing shes par
85b4(phal chen): gyur to// sems kyi skad cig re la yang rmi lam lta bu'i rnam par 'phrul pa yang dag par bstan pa'i sgo dag nas yang dag parabaskul ba byeng bar gyur to// sems kyi skad cig re re la yang
85b5(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba steng re re'i phan sa thams cad du skye ba dang 'chi 'pho ba yang dag par bstan pa 'i ske dag nas yang dag par skul pa byed par gyur te// sems
85b6(phal chen): kyi snying cig re re la yang 'jig rten gyi rdul shin tu phra ba srid kyi byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad shin tu bstan pa'i sgo dag nas yang dag par skul bar gyur to// sems kyi skad cig re
85b7(phal chen): la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'bam klas pa thams cad rab tu bskyod pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi yon tan rab tu brjod cing rnam par 'phrul pa'i sgo ngag nas yang dag par skul ba byed
85b8(phal chen): bar gyur to// sems kyi skad cig re re la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad yongasu dag pa rab pa dang / smon lam rgya mam thams cad rag bsgrag
86a1(phal chen): sgo dag nas yang dag par bskul ba byed par gyur to// sems kyi skad cig re re la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'gro ba thams cad kyi nges pa'i tshig dang / 
86a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi gsung gi yan lag rnam par bstan cing brjod pa'i sgo ngaganas/ yang dag par skul ba byed par gyur to// sems kyi skad cig re re la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi sa
86a3(phal chen): rgyas kyi chos kyi sprin thams cad kyi char dbab pa'i sgo dganas yang dag par skul ba byed par gyur to// sems kyi skad cig re re la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten
86a4(phal chen): gyi khamasu chos kyi dbyings snang bas rgyas par rnam par 'phrul pa 'i mthu'i sgo dag nas yang dag par skul ba byed par gyur to// sems kyi skad cig re re la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul
86a5(phal chen): shin tu phra ba sred kyi/ sangs rgyas kyi skus chos kyi dbyings pa/ nga bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa dang / 2do thams cad kyi sgo dag nas yang dag par skul ba byed par gyur to// 
86a6(phal chen): sems kyi skad cig re re la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho thams cad na byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po rab tu gnas pa'i sgod gnas yang
86a7(phal chen): dag par bskul ba byed par gyur to// de lta bu'i chos kyi dbyings rgyas par bkang ste/ sems can rnams kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du yang dag par skul ba byed cing / 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas
86a8(phal chen): pa dag tu rab tu bdal te/ zhing re re yang sems kyi skad cig re re laM/ sems can ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi ngan song gi rgyud du gtogs pa'i sdug bsngal thams cad ni rab tu zhi bar byed do// 
86b1(phal chen): sems can phyin ci lag la nges pa ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra bslang ni yang dag par nges pa'i phung po la rab tu 'god do// sems can ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snang ni dge ba dang yid du 'ong ba dang / mtho ris su skyes pa la
86b2(phal chen): rab tu 'god do// sems can ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba skad ni nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi sa la rab tu 'god do// sems can ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyeng ni dge ba'i bshes bsnyen bkur ba'i bsod
86b3(phal chen): nams kyi tshogs la rab tu 'god do// zhing de dag re rer yang sems can ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed ni sngan chad ma skyed pa'i byang chub kyi sems skye bar byed do// zhing de dag re rer yang sems can ri rab kyi
86b4(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba srad/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa phyir mi ldo ga pa yang dag par thob pa la yang dag par skul lo// zhing de dag re rer yang sems can ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed / 
86b5(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi spyan chos thams cad kun na sa sdang zhing gzigs pa la yongasu sbyangs te/ rab tu 'gro da // zhing de dag re rer yang sems can ri rab kyi rdul shin du pra
86b6(phal chen): srang stobs thams cad kyis rab tu gnas pa dang / ye shes kyi tshogs zad mi shes pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag par bya ba'i smon lam rgya mtsho la rab tu 'god do// zhing de dag re rer yang
86b7(phal chen): sems can ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyi gdung dang rgyud yang dag par 'thung ba'i gnas rgya mtsho rnam par spyod pa la rab tu 'gong ngo // byang dub sems pa
86b8(phal chen): de dag 'od zer gyi sgo thams cad ras kyang / tshig su bcad pa 'di lta bu dag byung bar gyur to// 'od zer thams cad sgo nas sgra 'byung ste// ji snyed byang chub spyod par 'jug pa dang // rgyal sras yon tan pur su
87a1(phal chen): gang yod pa'i// dbyangs kyis phyogs rnams kun tu bkang zhing sgeg/ bskal pa rgya mtshor skyo med spyad pa skyed// sdug bsngal kun las 'gre ba kun 'grel kyang // yid la skye med
87a2(phal chen): zhum pa gang yang med// 'di'i tshul la rgyal sras rab tu zhugs// chos kyi sgo rnams kun la rab skyed cing // tshul 'dir bskal pa rgya mtsho zad par byed// mtha' mang dpung med lhag ma gang yang med// de dag chas
87a3(phal chen): nyid zhi ba rab tu sgrog/ dus gsum rgyal ba'i smon lam gang yod pa// rgyal sras de dag 'gro la phan don du// de dag thams cad ma lus yongs sbyong // de dag spyod pa'i rgyan ni 'di 'da'o// rgyal bkun gyi
87a4(phal chen): 'khor du nyer phyin te// phyogs rnams kun na gzugs brnyan lus 'chang zhing // rgyal sras ye shes rgya mtsho'i blo gros can// de ngag chos nyid zhir 'jug 'di 'dra'o// 'od zer sde rnams ra rer mtha
87a5(phal chen): yas pa'i// bsam yas ning rnams de dag rab tu 'jug/ sgro da pas mig ni kun nas yongs dag ste// rgyal sras de dag spyod yul 'di yin no// ska rtse gcig tu de dag rab gnas shing / 
87a6(phal chen): zhing rnams dbyings kun kun nas bskyod bas kyang // sems can rnams la 'jigs par mi byed de// sa 'di rnam dag tshul 'chang dag gi'o// tshul rnams kun la bsam gyis mi khab lus// ro dag kun tu
87a7(phal chen): zhing rnams sna tshogs sprul// skad cig sems la 'chi 'pho skye ba snang // rgyan 'di sems la chags med rnams kyi'o// dus gsum bskal pa gang yod ma lus par// skad cig gcig gis thams
87a8(phal chen): cad rab tu ston// rgyu ma lta bu lus med dngos kyang med// de 'dra'i chos nyid chags med blos rdog so// bzang po'i spyod pa mchog la zhugs pa rnams// 'gro ba kun la yid du 'ong ba'i lus/ 
87b1(phal chen): rgyal sras de dag chos nyid 'di yin te// 'od zer kun gyi sgo nas dbyangs kyang sgrog/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' mtha' dang dpung med pa de dag/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul la rnam par
87b2(phal chen): spyod pas rnam par 'phrul pa thob par bya ba'i phyir/ smin mtshams kyi mdzod spu nas// 'od zer chen po byang chub sems dpa' thams cad ye shes kyi snang bas phyogs rnam par ston pa'i snying po zhes bya ba rab tu
87b3(phal chen): bkye'o// 'od zer rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog sgron ma sprin du 'dal ba/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du rab tu snang ba de byung nas/ tshul thams cad kyi phyogs 'bum klas pa rab tu snang bar byas te/ 
87b4(phal chen): phyogs thams cad kyi dbyings rgya mtsho rnams rab tu snang bar bas nas/ sems can rgya mtsho rnams rab tu snang bar byas te/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad rab tu bstan nas
87b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi zhing mang po thams cad rab tu bskyod pa'i rgyun gyi tshul thams cad kyis rab tu bskyod nas/ sangs rgyas kyi sprin 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba srad
87b6(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba thams cad dang mnyam pa dag tu rab tu spros nas/ sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa dang mos pa ji lta ba rgya mtsho dag tu/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo'i
87b7(phal chen): sngar gyi cha dus gsum gyi rdul shin tu phra ba dang mnyam pa bab ste/ dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rgya mtsho rab tu bstan nas/ sems can thams cad ma lus par 'khor ba
87b8(phal chen): thams cad las rab tu gdon pa rabya ba'i per mos pa ji bzhin du 'byung ba dang 'thun pa'i sprin gyi char rab tu dbab pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi smon lam ma lus pa'i sprin gyi bar rab tu
88a1(phal chen): dbab pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i 'khor dag tu dga' bar phrad pa bas nas/ bcom ldan 'das la g.yas pags
88a2(phal chen): su bskor byabs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar pad mo chen po rkub rin po che thams cad las bsgrubs pa nang rim nor bu'i rgyal po'i mdzod sna tshogs las bas pa/ lo ma rin po che thams cad kyi
88a3(phal chen): 'bebs pa/ ze ba'i phreng ba'i rgyan spos rin po che thams cad las bas pa/ snying po 'dzam+bu chu klung gi gser gyi tshon gyis rab tu mdzes par bris pa/ 'od kyi 'khor rnam par dag cing 'od zer gyi dra bas rnar
88a4(phal chen): par snang bar byas pa'i sprin dang ldan pa/ rgyan thams cad rab tu 'byung ba/ sems kyi skad cig la sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa mtha' yas pa ston pa'i sgra rab tu 'byung ba/ nor bu'i
88a5(phal chen): rgyal po mtha' yas pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi sku'i gzugs brnyan gyi sprin gyis thams cad du gang bar byed pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / sngon lam thams cad rab tu
88a6(phal chen): ston pa'i dbyangs 'byin par gyur te byung // pad+ma chen po de thung ba'i rjes la byang chub sems dpa' chos thams cad la pham med pa'i dbyangs shes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten gyi khams
88a7(phal chen): rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyeng dang lhan cig tu bcom ldan 'das kyi mdzod spu de nyid nas byung ste/ bcom ldan 'das la lan du mar g.yas phyogasu bskor ba bas nas/ bcom ldan 'das la phag 'tshal te

88b1(phal chen): thams cad la pham pa med pa'i dbyangs chos kyi dbyings rgya che zhing tshad med pas rab tu dga' ba'i shugs shin tu skyes pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi spyod yul gyi rjesu song ba'i ye shes can// sangs rgyas kyi
88b2(phal chen): chos kyi sku rgya mtsho bsam gyis mi khyab pa la rab tu zhugs pa'i mthu dang ldan pa/ zhing 'bam klas pa thams cad kyi de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi zhabs kyi drung du phyin pa/ baspu thams cad las sprul pa'i
88b3(phal chen): sprin zad mi shes pas kun tu khebs par byed pa/ sems kyi skad cig thams cad la dmigs pa thams cad chos kyi dbyings kun tu sbyar ba/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad la dus gsum khab par byed pa'i
88b4(phal chen): spyod yul gyis rnam par spyod pa/ phyogs thams cad kyi de ba zhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis brlabs 'chang ba/ tinge'i dza na thams cad la rab tu 'jog cing phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug
88b5(phal chen): par ti 'dzin dang / rnam par thar pa la rnam par spyod pa/ sangs rgyas kyi yon tan rgya mtsho mtha' yas pa thams cad dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi lus dang ldan pas de bzhin gshegs pa'i
88b6(phal chen): rdzu 'phrul dang / rnam par 'phrul pa mtha' dang dpung med pa la rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smraso// sangs rgyas sku ni chos kyi dbyings kyis gsal// 'gro ba kun la rgyal ba mngon sum
88b7(phal chen): ste/ ji ltar mos pa'i sems can rgyas bkang nas// snying po byang chub de la rgyal ba bzhugs// zhing rnams kun gyi rdul phran mchog snyed kyi// rgyal ba spu re kun la rab bzhugs te// bang chub snrelas dpa'
88b8(phal chen): 'khor gyis kun nas bskor// kun kyang bzang po'i spyod pa mchog ston to// spu gcig rtsel zhing mang rgya mtsho ste// byang chub snying por pad+mo gdan la bzhugs// chos dbyings rgya cher thams cad kur bkang
89a1(phal chen): sde spu rnams kun la rnam par 'phrul bsten// ning rnams re re dag na rab bzhugs shing // zhing rnams 'bam klas kun tu rgyas mdzad pas// phyogs bcu'i byang chub sems

89a3(phal chen): ribyings 'byam klas rtag tu rgyas par 'gangs// zhing rnams thams cad gzugs brnyan rab tu ston// chos dbyings rdul rnams ye shes spyod yul can// kun kyang bzang po'i spyod la rab tu gnas// sangs

89a5(phal chen): rnams kun tu bskal pa rgya mtshor spyod// rgya mtshor chos la rnam par snang bar spyod// de dag rgyal ba'i sa rnams rgya ma tsher nugs// sangs rgyas chos rnams gzhan dang gzhan 'byung

89b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas ye shes shin tu zab// dus rnams kun tu de 'thung ste// chos dbyings thug su chud pas na// 'jig rten mgon zhes rab tu brjod// yang dag sangs rgyas chos kyi sku// 'dres pa med cing gnas pa med/

89b4(phal chen): pa'i sku dag las// mi zad sangs rgyas sprul pa'i rnams// zhing rnams kun tu rabasgrog cing // chos kyi rgya mtsho shin tu ston/ spu rnams re re kun nas kyang // phyogs bcur 'od zer dra ba dag
89b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas gsung ni rab 'byin cing // gdul dka' thams cad rnam par 'dul// sangs rgyas 'od zer sgo rnams nas// sgra dbyangs zab mo rtag tu 'byung // sangs rgyas yon tan rgya
89b6(phal chen): meche ni// bang chub sems dpa'i spyod yul// sangs rgyas chos kyi 'khor lo dag/ mtha' dang dpung med rab tu sgor// ye shes zab mos shes bya ba// rgya chen po gsu rab tu ston// 'jig rten khams
89b7(phal chen): rnams thams cad du// rnam par 'phrul pa gzhan dang gzhan// chos kyi dbyings rnams kun bkang zhing // yang dag sangs rgyas ston pa mdzad// sku rnams rer kun las kyang // zhing rnams kun gyi rdul
89b8(phal chen): mnyam pa// sangs rgyas sems cad mnyam phyung zhing // rnam par 'phrul po rab tu ston// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chos rgya mtsho rnam par snang ba'i blo gros kyis// sangs rgyas kyi mthus phyogs bcur
90a1(phal chen): rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smras// chos kyi dbyings rnams kun khyab par// sangs rgyas sku ni rnam par mdzes// rgya chen gsum ni rab byung ba/

90a3(phal chen): kun la mngon// sems can thams cad bsam pa bzhin// thams cad gzigs pas sangs rgyas kyi// rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad mthong // mtha' yas 'od mnga' sangs rgyas sprin// chos rnams
90a4(phal chen): rgya mtsho'i 'brug kyang sgrog/ ye shes rnams rgyu'i tshul bzhin du// rgyal ba'i sras rnams de la 'jug/ 'jug pa rnams la 'byung ba med// 'byung ba yod par rnam par bstan// gang la
90a5(phal chen): sangs rgyas bzhugs pa yi// chos rnams 'byung ba na mkha' bzhin// 'obo dang gnas pa mi mnga' ste// 'on kyang rgyal ba kun na snang // sangs rgyas chos kyi dbyings las byung //

90a7(phal chen): sprin// bsam pa kun la rab tu byung // yang dag sangs rgyas rnams kun tu// sems can rgya mtsho 'dul ba mdzad// 'jig rten khams rnams thams cad kyi// snying po byang chub kun na snang // 'khor
90a8(phal chen): rgya mtsho thams cad na// zhing rnams kun gyis rnam par mdzes// sangs rgyas kun gyi sku dag la// yon tan rgya mtsho zad mi shes// sangs rgyas yon tan mtha' yas te// de dag yon tan zad pa
90b1(phal chen): med/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' smos 'od 'phro ba'i rgyan zla ba'i 'od kyis// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis// phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshig su bcad ba 'di dag smraso// bsam gyis
90b2(phal chen): mi khab sangs rgyas sar// byang chub sems dpa' gang bzhugs pa// de dang de dag sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul thams cad mthong // ye shes lus kyis zhugs pa rnams// zhing kun rdul gyi sbub su yang / 
90b3(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang // bdag nyid lus kyang der mthong ngo // gzugs brnyan zhing rnams thams cad dang // sangs rgyas kun gyi spyan sngar 'byung // kun tu byin gyis rlabs rnams dang / 
90b4(phal chen): rnam par 'phrul pa rab tu ston// kun tu bzang po'i smon lam dang // spyod pa gang gis rnam sbyangs pa// de dag ning rnams thams cad du// sangs rgyas kun gyi rnam 'phrul mthong / 
90b5(phal chen): kun tu mnyam pa nyid gyur cing // kun tu lus kyis rab gnas te// ye shes lus kyi rjes song nas// sangs rgyas spyod yu zhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas ye shes zhugs pa'i
90b6(phal chen): rnams// chos kyi dbyings la rnam par mdzes// sangs rgyas kun gyi sgra dag tu// rgya mtsho'i zhing la rab tu 'jug/ sangs rgyas kun gyi zhing dag tu// byin gyi rlabs rnams rab bstan pas/ 
90b7(phal chen): gzhan dang gzhan gyi lus dag dang / ming gis kun na rab tu gnas// byang chub snying por rnam 'phrul dang // byang chub mngon par 'chang rgya zhing // chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bdag/ skad cig sem
90b8(phal chen): kyis ston pa byed// zhing rnams 'bam klas thams cad dang // bskal pa bye ba bsam yas dag/ byang chub sems dpa' mnyam bzhag rnams// skad cig sems kyis rnam par ston// sangs rgyas
91a1(phal chen): zhing rnams thams cad na// byang chub sems dpa'i sprul pa rnams// sangs rgyas sku la rnam spyod kyang // mtha' ma rnyed par mi rung // de nas byang chub sems dpa' seng ge'i
91a2(phal chen): 'od zer snang bas mthu 'byin pa'i blo gros kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigasu bcad pa 'di dag smra so// sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad kyi// chos
91a3(phal chen): kyi 'khor lo rab tu 'khor// chos dbyings tshul rnams thams cad kyang // sangs rgyas sprin gyis mngon tu yog/ 'jig rten khams rnams rgya mtsho dang // phyogs bcu kun na gang yod pa// thams cad kun tu
91a4(phal chen): 'khor lo 'khor// de ni smon lam rnam 'bral ba'o// 'khor rnam sa rgya mtsho rgya che ba// gzhan dang gzhan gyi ming dag gis// zhing rnams gnas pa kun tu yang // chos kyi 'khor lo kun
91a5(phal chen): tu 'khor// rnam par snang mdzad byin gyi rlabs// zhing rnams rgya mtsho kun tu yang // kun tu bzang po'i smon lam dag/ rjod cing zhing rnams kun tu 'byung // zhing kun rdul la
91a6(phal chen): sku'i rnams// thams cad chos char rab tu 'bebs// 'dres pa med cing 'byung ba med// 'jig rten dag na rnam par mdzes// bskal pa bye ba grangs med par/ zhing kun rdul phran sbubs dag tu/ 
91a7(phal chen): rnam par snang ba mdzad pa'i gsung // sngon gyi spyod pa rab tu sgrog/ zhing rnams thams cad rdul snyed kyi// 'od zer dra ba phyogs bcun// sangs rgyas 'od zer kun sgo nas// byang chub mchog par sam
91a8(phal chen): can 'dul// kun tu ma 'dres sku dag gis// chos dbyings yongasu rab gsal te// 'gro rnams 'dul ba ji bzhin du// gzugs kyi skur yang rab tu mthong // dus gsum zhing rnams thams cad kyi/ 
91b1(phal chen): mgon po ji skad bzhugs pa rnams// de dag kun gyi mtshan kyang sgrog/ sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul la ltos// da ltar byung dang 'das pa dang // sangs rgyas gang rnams ma byon pa// de dag kun gyi bsam yas
91b2(phal chen): chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu grag/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi yon tan gyi mdzod mi zad pa'i dpal gyi gzi brjid mar mes sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis// phyogs bcur rnam par
91b3(phal chen): bltas te/ de'i tshe tshig su bcang ba 'di dag spros// gang gis byang chub sems dpa' yi// ye shes tshogs 'di kun non cing // ye shes rtogs pa rnyed pa'i rnams// de dag 'di yi tshul la zhugs/ 
91b4(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings dang mnyam pa'i dbyangs// zhing rnams kun tu rab tu 'byung // sangs rgyas kun gyi spyod yul te// byang chub sems dpa'i tshad du brjod// skad cig re re'i sems kun la/ 
91b5(phal chen): chos kyi dbyingasu rnam par rgyu// de bzhin nyid la gnas shing brta na// chos rnams rgya mtsho kun la zhugs// rgyan gyi ba rol phyin pa rnams// bskal pa bye ba bsapa ya su// sangs
91b6(phal chen): rgyas thams cad sku dag tu// zhing rnams kun na gnas shing spyod// rdul rnams re re'i stengs nas kyang // chos rnams kun ni rab tu 'byung // zhing rnams kun kyang khab par byed// ye shes chags
91b7(phal chen): med spyod yulo// sangs rgyas thams cad spyod yul du// lus pa med par kun bkang zhing // rnam par 'phrul pa'i rnam spyod pas// sangs rgyas spyod yul rnams la zhugs// sangs rgyas kun gyi
91b8(phal chen): rjes stegs dbyangs// chos kyi dbyings ni rab sgrog pa// chos dbyings rjesu shes pa'i rnams// dbyangs kyi rgya mtsho rnams la spyod// bskal pa rgya mtshor ma 'dres par// sgra dang dbangs
92a1(phal chen): rnams te shin tu sgrog/ dus rnams thams cad shes pas gsal// dbyangs kyis de dag sa la zhugs// sgra'i shes la rmongs pa med// sems can sgra yang spyong
92a2(phal chen): yul te// thams cad mkhyen pa kun gyi yang // rnam par 'phrul pa'i dbyangs sheso// sa nas sar yang phyin gyur cing // stobs kyi sa la rab gnas te// bskal pa ba bar spyad pas na// chos nyid 'di
92a3(phal chen): rab tu 'jug/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' ye shes kyi 'od zer shes rab kun nas sgron ma'i blo gros kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis// phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i mtshigasu
92a4(phal chen): bcad pa 'di dag smraso// gang la sangs rgyas bzhugs pa yi// chos rnams de dag mtshan nyid med// ye shes sa ni thob pa'i rnams// 'jig rten gtso bo rab tu mthong // shes rab snang ba'i
92a5(phal chen): kun 'od can// byang chub sems dpa' mnyam bzhag rnams/ sangs rgyas thams cad kun gyi yang // sku yi rnam pa ra 'phrul la zhugs// chos kyi dbyings la rnam spyad cing // lus
92a6(phal chen): kyi dngos la rab 'jug ste// zab mo'i chos rnams rtogs gyur nas// smon lam dag gis yang dag byung // bsod nams rgya mtshos byung gyur cing // ye shes sa la rnam par gnas// chos la rnam spyod
92a7(phal chen): khong du chud// spyod pa'i mchog la rab tu spyod// sangs rgyas zhing rnams thams cad kyi// sangs rgyas kun gyi drung dag tu// chos kyi dbyings la spyad pas na// rang bzhin lus ni rab tu mthong // shing
92a8(phal chen): 'bam klas thams cad du// bskal pa bye ba bsam ya su// thams cad gzigs pa'i chos kyi rnams// rgya mtsho kun la rab tu spyod// bdag mthong bas ni lus dang rdul// gcig tu 'dres par
92b1(phal chen): mngon pa rla bas/ ma skyes mtshan nyid med pa ste// zhing rnams kun du'ang rnam par mdzes// 'jig rten kun gyi bsam 'thun par// sems can kun la mngon sum du// lus kyi sprin ni bstan bas
92b2(phal chen): shing // byang chub don tu sems can 'dul// sangs rgyas thams cad mthu yis na// byang chub sems dpar brjod pa ste// gang gis mgon po mthong ba yi// rgyal ba'i'abyin rlabs shin tu zab
92b3(phal chen): mgon po je snyed gang bzhugs pa'i// byin rlabs mtha' dang dpung med de// chos dbyings rab tu gang byas nas// byang chub sems dpa' rnar 'chang rgya// de nas byang chub sems dpa' me tog kun nas 'ong
92b4(phal chen): 'phro gtsug bud rab tu 'phang bas// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi sa brlabs kyis// phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smos// zhing rnams kun tu
92b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi// gsung gi dkyil 'khor sgra 'byin te/ chos kyi dbyings rnams gang byas nas// yon tan sprin ni rab tu brjod// yang dag sangs rgyas chos kyi sku// rnam
92b6(phal chen): ngag dmakha' 'dra ba ste// gzugs kyi sku yang rab bstan cing // chos nyid 'di la shin tu 'jug/ dga' dang mos pa'i shugs rnams dang // sangs rgyas stobs rnams thams cad la// rab tu
92b7(phal chen): gnas shing de dag ni// de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes 'jug/ shes rab chung ngus ches 'di dag // kun nas shes par mi nus te// ye shes mig ni rab sbyangs shing // 'di'i tshul la 'jug par
92b8(phal chen): 'gyur// rabag tu gnas dang byin rlabs dang // chos kun rnam par spyad pa dang // rab tu 'jug dang ldan pa yi// mnyam pa nyid la rag tu zhugs// chos rnams mtha' yas glong gi rnams// chos kun
93a1(phal chen): mtshan nyid rnams la te// kun mkhyen nyid la rabazhugs shing // chos kyi rgya mtsho kun la spyod// sangs rgyas zhing na kun 'khod cing // thams cad kun na rnam par mdzes// 'o
93a2(phal chen): ba med cing 'phos pa meng // sangs rgyas chos nyid de 'dra'o// gzugs brnyan 'dra ba'i sku rnams ni// sems can rgya mtsho'i nang na snang // mos pa ci 'dra yod pa'i rnams// de bzhin mgon po kun gyis mthong // 
93a3(phal chen): kun tu bzang po'i smon lam dang // spyod pa mang po sus sbyangs pa// de dag thams cad ba spu la'ang // rnam 'phrul gzhan dang gzhan dag mthong // lus kyi rnams ni re res kyang // chos kyi dbyings rnam
93a4(phal chen): kun tu khyab// 'khor lo kun na 'khor ba ste// chos kyi 'khor lo bsam mi khyab// de nas byang chub sems dpa' 'od zer dang // gzi ba rjid mi zad pa'i rgyal po blo gros kyis// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi
93a5(phal chen): rlabs kyis// phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te// de'i tshe tshi gsu bcad pa 'di dag smras// sangs rgyas sku ni thams cad nas// 'od zer sprin mang phyogs rnams bcur// kha dog
93a6(phal chen): mtha' yas 'bar ba'i 'od// sems can bsam pa kun la 'bro// sangs rgyas zhing rnams thams cad kyi// snying po byang chub kun na bzhugs// bdud rnams thams cad rab btul te// 'khor
93a7(phal chen): gyi nang na rnam par mdzes// thams cad rdul na'ang ma 'dres par// 'od zer dkyil 'khor rgyas par 'gengs// phyogs rnams gzhan dang gzhan lam tu// zhing gi rgyud rnams rab tu ston// zhing gi
93a8(phal chen): rnams ni rgya mtsho'i grong // phyogs kyi rnams kyang kun tu gnon// zhing rnams thang chen mnyam zhing dag/ in dra nI lar kun nas gnas// spyi'u tshugs dag dang snrel zhi dang // pad+mo'i dbyibs
93b1(phal chen): dang khang khrung dang // dkyil 'khor 'khor lo'i khad par du// gzugs rnams kun gyis rab tu gnas// chos kyi dbyings rnams gar byin par// thug pa med par 'gram 'das ba// de dag kun gyi 'khor rnamasu/ 
93b2(phal chen): shin du bstan pa'i chos 'byung ngo // de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku dbyings na// 'khod pa'i shing rnams bsam mi khyab// de dag kun tu chos nyid 'di// 'jig rten mgon po rnams kyang sngon// tha dad med pa 'tsho
93b3(phal chen): dbyings// chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu 'khor// gcig gi tshul gyi rnam pa yis// chos bstan pa ni kun tu 'byung // sangs rgyas gsung gi dkyil 'khor ni// tshul rnams thams cad rab tu brjod// dang brgya
93b4(phal chen): mtsho'i tshul dag gis// mi zang tshul rnams rab tu bstan// / sangs rgyas zhing rnams kun na yang // rgyal ba rnams ni mig yor 'drar// snying po byang chub rnams na snang // 'byung ba dag kyang
93b5(phal chen): yod pa min// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi dbyingasu 'od 'phro ba rnam par snang ba 'thung ba'i blo gros kyis// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis// phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ 
93b6(phal chen): de'i tshe tshigasu bcad pa 'di dag smras// blta zhing blta zhing sangs rgyas rnams// sku gzugs bsam gyis mi khyab ste// dga' ba rgya mtsho kun kyang 'byung // chos kyi shugs ni rab tu 'phel// mtshan
93b7(phal chen): rab kun nas sangs rgyas rnams// phyogs bcu kun tu rab tu 'byung // rdul rnams kun tu 'jug pa yis// sangs rgyas sprin kyang de bzhin bstan// skad cig skad cig sems kun la// sangs rgyas 'od ni
93b8(phal chen): dpal gyis 'bar// rnam 'phrul gzhan dang gzhan dag gis// zhing rnams rgya mtsho kun na snang // byang chub sems dpa' shes rab che// rgya mtsho chos las 'byung ba rnams// sangs rgyas kun gyis byin rlabs
94a1(phal chen): pa/ 'di'i yul la rnam par spyod// kun tu bzang po'i smon lam la// gang rnams shin tu gnas gyur pa// de dang de rnams ning drug tu// sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul kun lal/ 
94a2(phal chen): ye shes zab mo rnam gnon cing // chos kyi dbyings la gzhol ba ni// mos pa rgya mtsho shes pa ste// smon lam kun gyis byung ba'o// sangs rgyas kun gyi sku dang gsung / chags pa mdal rab tu zhugs
94a3(phal chen): spyod pa gzhan dang gzhan dag gis// spyod yul kun kyang khong du chud// sangs rgyas kun gyi sku gnas shing // ye shes spyod yul gyur pa'i rnams// chos kyi dbyings la rab brtson pa// rgyal ba rnams
94a4(phal chen): kyis gnon to// skad cig sems kyis zhing gi rnams// sangs rgyas zhing gi rdul mnyam pa// de dag chos nyid ji bzhin du// rdul gcig stang du rnam par sbyong // zhing rnams ji snyed
94a5(phal chen): thams cad na// zhing gi rnam 'phrul gang yod pa// chos nyid 'a de la zhugs pa'i rnams// zhing gcig du ni sdud pa byed// de nas byang chub sems dpa' stobs dang / brtson 'grus
94a6(phal chen): chags pa med pa'i blo gros kyis// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis// phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigasu bcad pa 'di dag smras// zhing rnams rgya mtsho thams cad du// de dag gsung
94a7(phal chen): ni zab mo 'byung // dbyangs kyi yan lag kun rgyas pa// chos kyi sprin gyi char 'bebs so// brjod pa rgya mtsho thams cad kyis// sems can kun gyi skad dag tu// sangs rgyas zhing rnams kun tu
94a8(phal chen): yang // chos rnams bstan pa rab tu 'byung // zhing rnams kun tu ma lus par// sangs rgyas rnam par 'phral mthong zhing // sangs rgyas gsung rnams thos pa dang // byang chub mchog phyir kun kyang
94b1(phal chen): 'jug/ rdul rnams re re'i sdeng nas kyang // chos kyi dbyings kyi phyogs tshul gyis// sangs rgyas zhing rnams kun bkang zhing // sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul sngon pa byed// chos kyi sku ni tha dad min/ 
94b2(phal chen): ra mkha' bzhin te chags pa med// gzugs kyi skur ni rnam dmigs pa// mig yor snang ba'i mtshan nyid do// mig yor yul la mi gnas te// na mkha' bzhin du dngos po med// mnyam pa nyid
94b3(phal chen): 'di rtogs gyur nas// ye shes rgya mtsho mthong bar 'gyur// sangs rgyas sku ni ma skyes te// gzung ba med cing byung ba med// nam mkha'i mnyam pa nyid dang mtshungs// gzung du med las 'di bstan to// 
94b4(phal chen): zhing rnams kun gyi sangs rgyas rnams// de dag spu gcig rtsel tsho gas// ye shes mig dang ldan pa yis// spu rnams kun tu rnam 'phrul mthong // rnam par snang mdzad smon lam ste/ 
94b5(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings ni kun bkang zhing // bla med chos kyi 'khor lo/ dag/ zhing rnams kun na rtag tu 'khor// ji ste bskal pa bsam yas par// spu rtse gcig tu rnam sbal pa// sangs
94b6(phal chen): rgyas kun gyis bshad mdzad kyang // de'i mtha' ni rnyed par dga'// ji ltar gling bzhi pa 'dir/ de bzhin gshegs pas rnam par sgrol pa'i snying po byang chub tu phyogs bcu nas// bang chub/ 
94b7(phal chen): sems dpa' rnams 'dus par gyur pa/ de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i gling bzhi pa thams cad kyi gling bzhi pa re rer yang / de bzhin gshegs pas rnam par sprul pa'i snying po byeng chub dag
94b8(phal chen): tu/ byang chub sems dpa' phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho byed pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kun nas 'dus par gyur to// 'di na ji lta ba de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi snying
95a1(phal chen): po byang chub de bzhin gshegs pas rnam par sprul pa dag tu/ kun nas 'dus pa'i byang chub sems dang 'di dag kyang chos nyid 'di kho na rab tu ston to// 
95a2(phal chen): shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo// sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba las/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o// / ma de nas bcom ldan
95a3(phal chen): 'das kyi spyan sngar/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po seng ge'i khri pad+mo'i snying po can de nyid la 'dug ste/ de'i tshe sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ ting 'dzin sangs rgyas thams cad
95a4(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku'i snying po zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi rjes song ba'i rang bzhin chos kyi dbyings kyi gzugs brnyan rnam par
95a5(phal chen): btags pa'i tshogs na mkha'i dbyings chags pa med cing / rgya che ba khyab par byed pa'i rang bzhin chos kyi dbyings rgya mtsho'i glong mnyam pa nyid kyi rjesu song zhing / shin tu 'dal ba'i cho ga
95a6(phal chen): chos thams cad kyi sgo'i dbyings ting 'dzin gyi dkyil 'khor yang dag par 'byung bas rgyas par 'gengs pa/ phyogs thams cad du yang dag par zhugs pa'i chos kyi dbyings kyi lus kyis kun nas yog
95a7(phal chen): par byas pa'i rang bzhin gyi snying po can dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas 'byung ba'i ye shes snang ba rgya mtsho'i klong / phyogs thams cad du sgro kun nas tshul rgya mtsho rnam par rig par byabs mngon tu yang dag
95a8(phal chen): par ston pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi stobs dang rnam par thar pas byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi lus rgyas par 'gengs pa'i snying po can/ zhing 'byam klas pa thams cad ma lus par
95b1(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings su 'jug pas rgyas par 'gengs pa'i ye shes dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi yon tan rgya mtsho thams cad yongasu grub par byed pa bskal pa thams cad du smon lam rgya mtshos rnam par snang bar
95b2(phal chen): byeng ba'i 'od can/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo ston cing rjod pa'i byin gyi rlabs la mnyam par bzhag par gyur to// ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos/ bcom
95b3(phal chen): ldan 'das kyi zhabs kyi drung du byang chub sems dpa'i ting 'dzin sangs rgyas thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku'i snying po zhes bya ba'i 'di la mnyam par bzhag pa de bzhin du/ 'jig rten
95b4(phal chen): gyi khams 'byam klas pa/ chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa/ na mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas gtugs pa/ phyogs rgya mtsho thams cad kyi khamasu gtogs pa/ dus gsum thams cad na yod pa'i sangs
95b5(phal chen): rgyas kyi zhing 'byung ba'i khams chos kyi dbyings rgya chen pos non pa'i rig su gtogs pa/ shin tu phra zhing bsgribs pa med pa dang / phyogs rgya chen po rgya mtsho thams cad snang
95b6(phal chen): ba 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i ri su gtogs pas rnam par non pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyan gyis rnam par gzigs pa sang sa rgyas kyi stobs thogs pa med pas chud pa/ chos kyi dbangs
95b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi sku thams cad kyi gzugs brlan rab tu snang bas/ chos kyi dbyings kyi rdul ma lus pa kun tu gtogs pa/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad du rgyas par gang ba'i 'jig rten gyi
95b8(phal chen): khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba dang mnyam bdag tu rdul phra mo re re la'ang zhing 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho rdul shin tu phra ba snod la rab tu zhugs nas/ zhing re re zhing yang de bzhin gshegs pa
96a1(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi rnams kyi rdub shin tu phra ba snyed la ragadu zhugs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa re ri'i gabs kyi drung du yang lus 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba sted kyis 'i
96a2(phal chen): 'dzin sangs rgyas thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku'i snying po zhes bya ba 'di la mnyam par bzhag go// byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos byang chub sems dpa'i ting 'dzin sangs
96a3(phal chen): rgyas thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku'i snying po zhes bya ba de la mnyam par bzhag pa'i rjes la/ de'i tshe phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'byam klas pa thams cad nas de bzhin gabye
96a4(phal chen): pa thams cad kyis zhal bstan to// yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sa ngas rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis 'di skad ces kyang bka' stsal te/ rigs kyi bu khyod de ltar byang chub sems dpa'i ting
96a5(phal chen): 'dzin sangs rgyas thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyi skur snying po 'di la mnyam par gzhog pa gso leg so// kye rgyal ba'i bu khyod la phyogs bcu'i
96a6(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa 'di dag thams cad kyang / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad 'di'i sngon gyi smon lam gyi byin gyis brlabs dang / khyod kyi sangs rgyas thams cad kyi
96a7(phal chen): smon lam dang / spyod pas yongs su dag pa'i yang mthus 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes rgya mtsho thams cad rnam par dbye ba dang / 
96a8(phal chen): chos thams cad kyi tshul gyi phyogs rgya mtsho ma lus par snang bar bya ba dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang ba rnam par dag par bya ba dang / chags pa
96b1(phal chen): med par 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa thams cad yong su gnan pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi yul thams cad la chags pa med par 'jug par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi 'khor thams cad
96b2(phal chen): kun nas rab tu brjod pa dang / chos kyi tshul gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad la zhugs pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid yongasu gzung ba dang / chos kyi snang ba thams cad kyi tshul rnam par blta ba dang / sems
96b3(phal chen): can gyi dbang po rgya mtsho thams cad yong su shes par bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung gi yan lag rgya mtsho'i dbyangs yongasu gzung ba'i phyir byin gyis rlob pa mdzad do// de nas sangs rgyas
96b4(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po la/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi stob sa la rab tu 'jug pa'i ye shes kyang nye bar bsgrub so// chos
96b5(phal chen): kyi dbyings mtha' dang dpung med pa la rab tu 'jug pa'i ye shes kyang nye bar bsgrub so// dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi dkyil 'a khor thams cad yang dag par 'byung ba'i ye shes kyang nye bar bsgrun
96b6(phal chen): so// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad 'jig pa dang 'du ba'i ye shes kyang nye bar bsgrubaso// chos kyi dbyings 'byam klas pa mtha' dang dpung med pa la 'jug pa'i ye shes kyang nye bar bsgrub so// sangs
96b7(phal chen): rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa zab mo tha mi dad pa dang / ting 'dzin thams cad la rnam par gnas pa'i ye shes kyang nye bar bsgrub so// byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi dbang po rgya mtsho la rab tu 'jug pa'i ya
96b8(phal chen): shes kyang nye bar bsgrub so// sems can thams cad kyi skad rgya mtsho dang chos kyi 'khor lo'i nges pa'i tshig gi ye shes kyang zhi bar bsgrub so// 'jig rten gyi khams mang po thams cad kyi rjesu song zhing chos kyi dbyings
97a1(phal chen): thams cad du lus yang dag par gzhol ba'i ye shes kyang nye bar bsgrub so// sangs rgyas kyi gsung gi yan lag dang sgra dbyangs kyang nye bar bsgrub so// ji ltar 'jig rten gyi khams
97a2(phal chen): 'di'i bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs kyi drung na 'dug pa la nye bar bsgrubs pa de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag dang rdul shin tu phra ba'i khongs na lus
97a3(phal chen): 'khod pa thams cad la yang nye bar bsgrub so// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ da ni 'di ltar ting 'dzin de nyid kyi chos nyid kyi chos nyid thob pa'i phyir ro// de nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyis sprul pa'i sangs rgyas
97a4(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das de dag gis phyag g.yas pa mtshan dang dpe byad bzang pos rnam par mdzes par brgyan pa/ 'od zer gyi dra ba'i me tog sna tshogs shin tu rgyas pa 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rnam par dag
97a5(phal chen): pa'i sprin 'gyed pa/ rin po che 'od 'phro ba thams cad kyi sprin gyi/ sa rnam par gsal bar gyur pa/ phyogs thams cad du spo sa 'od 'phro ba'i sprin gyi 'od kyis rnam par snang ba/ sangs rgyas
97a6(phal chen): thams cad kyi gsung gi yan lag gi dkyil 'khor gyi rjesu sgra 'byin pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul pa dang / khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba yang dag par ston pa/ byang chub sems dpa' 'das pa dang / 
97a7(phal chen): ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba rnams kyi kun tu bzang po'i smon lam gyi dkyil 'khor rab tu snang ba rnam par ston pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo'i snang ba yang dag par ston pa/ 
97a8(phal chen): dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gzugs brnyan 'byung ba rnams brkang ste/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyi bor bzhag go// 'dir ji lta ba de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams
