97b1(phal chen): rgya mche thams cad dang rdul shin tu phra ba'i khongs na yod pa thams cad du yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhabs kyi drung dag tu byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyi bo la phyag rgya mtsho'i sprin rnams rab tu bzhag
97b2(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po la sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis reg ma thag tu de nas de'i med la ting 'dzin de las ldang ba'i sgo rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba skad
97b3(phal chen): dus gsum thams cad du sems kyi skad cig re ra la ting 'dzin las ldang ba'i ye shes ma 'dres pa la mkhas pa dang / ting 'dzin las ldang ba'i byin gyi rlabs kyi sgo chos kyi dbyings dang / dus gsum du
97b4(phal chen): mnyam pa'i rdul thams cad kyi sgo dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'a ngas pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba thams cad kyi sgo dang / sems can ma lus pa'i gnas thams cad dang mnyama'i
97b5(phal chen): sems can thams cad kyi sems rgya mtsho la 'jug pa'i sgo dang / sems can thams cad kyi lus dang mang gi 'khor lo la sa ldang ba'i sgo dang / sems can phyogs mtshams thams cad
97b6(phal chen): du chos kyi dbyings rnam par 'byed pa'i sgo dang / rdul shin tu phra ba thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi sku'i sprin mtha' dang dpung med par 'bam klas pa'i sgo dang / chos kyi tshul rgya mtsho thams cad rab tu bsdar
97b7(phal chen): pa'i sgo dag nas langs par gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po ting 'dzin lase langs ma thag tu/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' de dag kyang so so re re zhing ting 'dzin rgya mtsho'i sgora'ijag
97b8(phal chen): rter gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snying la rab tu zhugs par gyur te// gzungs rgya mtsho'i sprin 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la yang rab tu zhugs par gyurapa/ 
98a1(phal chen): chos kyi tshul rgya mtsho'i sprin 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la yang rab tu zhugs par gyur to// so so yang dag par rig pa'i tshul rgya mtsho'i sprin 'jig rten gyi
98a2(phal chen): khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra bsnyed la yang rab tu zhugs par gyur to// spyod pa rgya mtsho'i sprin 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la yang rag tu zhugs par gyur to// chos kyi dbyings
98a3(phal chen): kyi phyogs su rnam par snang zhing de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes snang ba'i yon tan gyi snying po can rgya mtsho'i sprin 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la yang rab tu zhugs par
98a4(phal chen): gyur to// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs dang / ye shes ma 'dres pa'i tshul rgya mtsho'i sprin 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la yang rab tu zhugs par gyur te// de
98a5(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ba spu'i rtse mo thams cad la zhing gzhan dang gzhan rgya mtsho'i sprin 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba skad la yang rab tu zhugs par
98a6(phal chen): gyur to// byang chub sems dpa' re re zhing dga' ldan gyi gnas nas 'pho ba dang / 'byung ba dang / byang chub tu rnam par 'tshang rgya ba dang / mya ngan las 'das pa bstan pa rgya mtsho'i sprin 'jig
98a7(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la'ang rab tu zhugs par gyur to// 'dir ji lta ba de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad yang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor
98a8(phal chen): rgya mtsho rnams dang rdul shin tu phra ba thams cad kyi khongs na yod pa kun tu yang byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho rnams rab tu zhugs par gyur te/ sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang byang chub sems dpa' kun tu
98b1(phal chen): bzang po'i ting 'dzin gyi chos nyid rab tu thob pas phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad ma lus par bag langs tsam du g.yos te/ rin po che thams cad kyis rab tu brgyan par gnas shing
98b2(phal chen): chos rgya mtsho thams cad kyi sgra yang shin tu grags par gyur te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho thams cad du yang nor bu'i rgyal po bcu'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab par gyur to// bcu gang zhe na/ 
98b3(phal chen): 'di lta ste/ nor bu'i rgyal po mtshan dang ldan pa'i gser dpal gyi rgyal la mching sa'i sprin char mngon par bab bo// 'di lnga ste/ nor bu'i rgyal po 'od kyis rnam par gsal bar byeng pa'i sprin char mngon
98b4(phal chen): bar bab bo// 'di lta ste/ nor bu'i rgyal po phyogs bcur rin po che'i 'khor lo rab tu 'grems pa'i sprin gyi char mdo na bar bab bo// 'di lta ste/ nor bu'i rgyal po byang chub
98b5(phal chen): sems dpa'i gzugs brnyan rin po che'i snying po'i sprin gyirma ra mngon par bab bo// 'di lta ste/ nor bu'i rgyal po sangs rgyas thams cad kyi mtshan gyi 'khor lo rab tu sgrog pa'i sprin
98b6(phal chen): gyi char mngon par ba'o// de rje/ nor bu'i rgyal po zhing rnam par snang bar byed cing snying po byang chub tu dpal rab tu 'bar ba'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab bo// 'di lta ste/ nor bu'i rgyal po phyogs bcur snang
98b7(phal chen): ba'i sprul pa 'gyed pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab bo// 'di lta ste/ nor bu'i rgyal po byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi yon tan gyi 'khor lo dang mthu rab tu grag par byed pa'i sprin gyi char
98b8(phal chen): mngon par bab bo// 'di lta ste/ nor bu'i rgyal po nyi ma'i dpal gyi gzi brjid kyi sprin gyi char mngon par bab po// 'di lta ste/ nor bu'i rgyal po rol mo'i sgra yid du 'ong bas phyogs thams cad khyab
99a1(phal chen): par byed pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab ste/ nor bu'i rgyal po'i sprin gyi char bcu po 'di dag mngon par bab par gyur to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi baspu'i sgo thams cad dang / 'od
99a2(phal chen): zer gyi sgo thams cad nas kyang tshig su bcad pa 'di dag byung bar gyur to// zhing rnams 'byam klas kun na kun tu bzang po de// pad+mo yid du 'ong la rab tu 'dug pa mthong // kun tu rnam 'phrul rnam pa 'di 'dra ston byed pa/ 
99a3(phal chen): ting 'dzin yul la 'jug pa mtha' dang dpung med do// lus rnams thams cad nas kyang kun tu bzang po de// sprul pa rab tu 'gyed cing chos dbyings rtag par 'gengs// ting 'dzin kun gyi tshul dang ming dang rnam
99a4(phal chen): 'phrul pa// thams cad dbyangs kyis chags pa med pa rgya che sgrog ting 'dzin thams cad gzhan dang gzhan gyi rnam 'phrul gyis// / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad zhabs kyi drung dag tu// rgyal
99a5(phal chen): ba kun gyi spyod yul yangs pa gang byas te// zhing rnams kun tu rnam par 'phrul pa mang po ston// zhing kun rgyal ba kun gyi zhabs drung ji bzhin du// de ltar zhing kun shin tu phra ba'i rdul phran
99a6(phal chen): / ting 'dzin rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad ma lus ston// rnam par snang mdzad smon lam dbyings la rab tu zhugs// kun tu bzang po'i lus ni na mkha'i mtshan nyid de// thams cad zhing la mi gan
99a7(phal chen): de bzhin nyid la gnas// lus kyi sprin ni 'gro ba kun dang mnyam par kun bkye zhing // sems can kun la bsam pa bzhin du de dag ston// sangs rgyas sku rnams kun la zhing rnams gang yod pa/ 
99a8(phal chen): mtha' dang dpung med kun la rab tu zhugs pa rnams// kun tu bzang po'i smon lam gnas pa dag la bstan// rnam par 'phrul pa 'di 'dra dam pa tshad kyang med// 'khor rnams rgya mtsho rdul bral mtha'
99b1(phal chen): dang dpung med pa// tshad med thams cad lus kyi nang du kun chub cing // dbyangs la zhing mang dra bar rnam 'tshang rgya ba ston// skad cig sems la bskal pa mang po de bzhin sngon// zhing rnams thams cad 'byam
99b2(phal chen): klas pa na rnam gnas shing // rnam par 'phrul ba dam pa ston par rab tu snang // phyogs rnams kun gyi zhing gi dbyings rnams ma lus spyod// kun tu bzang po de la rnam lha kun kyang mthong // rgyal ba kun
99b3(phal chen): gyi yon tan ye shes stobs la zhugs// ting 'dzin sa ni tshul rnams kun gyis rab tu mnon// chos rnams 'byam klas gzhan dang gzhan la rab tu zhugs// rang gi byang chub spyod pa sngan chad spyad pa
99b4(phal chen): sngor// de ltar zhing rnams kun tu bsam yas rnam 'phrul ba// phyogs rnams rgya che kun tu bkang ste rab tu bstan// tite 'dzin rnams 'jug pa rab tu bstan pa'i phyir// rgyal ba'i
99b5(phal chen): 'od zer sprin las yon tan legs sgra 'byung // de nas byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor yod pa thams cad sangs rgyas kyi mthus thal mo sbyar te// byang chub sems dpa' kun tu
99b6(phal chen): bzang po la lta zhing dbyangs kyi nga ro gcig tu de'i tshe tshigs bcang ba 'di dag smraso// rgyal ba thams cad chos las skyes pa ste// smon lam kun gyis sangs rgyas rab tu byung // de bzhin nyid mnya
99b7(phal chen): na mkha'i snying po ste// chos kyi sku yis rnam par rab tu mdzes// zhing rnams 'byam klas kun la bzhugs med kyang // kun tu bzang po'i 'khor rnams kun na snang // phyogs bcu kun tu
99b8(phal chen): yon tan grags pa khyab// ye shes rgya mtsho rab tu snang ba mnga'// rgyal ba thams cad sku thob phyir spyod pa// phyogs bcu'i yon tan rgya mtsho yod pa rnams// rdul sbubs kun tu de dag chung
100a1(phal chen): byas shing // zhing rnams kun tu rnam par rab tu mdzes// zhing rnams kun gyi rgyal ba'i zhabs drung na// rgyal sras ting 'dzin dang spyod pa dang / chos rnams kun la spyod
100a2(phal chen): cing gnas pa'i rnams// rdul dang mnyam pa'i bskal par kun kyang snang // chos kyi dbyings rnams lus kyis khyab byas shing // zhing rnams 'bum klas kun la shin tu zhugs// sems can rgya mtsho'i
100a3(phal chen): don du de spyod cing // rdul phran kun la chos kyi dbyingasu zhugs// chos kyi dbyings la de ltar zhugs nas kyang // rdul phran kun la mi zad tha ma dang // na mkha'i dbyings ni lus kyis gang byas shing // rgyal
100a4(phal chen): ngi'i chos rnams yangs pa rab tu ston// yon tan rgya mtsho 'od kun gzhal du med// rnam yangs stobs chen 'od ce ra yon tan sprin// 'gro ba rgya mtsho'i don du spyod byed cing / 
100a5(phal chen): rgyal ba'i spyod lam gzhal du med pa sngon// gang gi don du bskal pa/ rgya mtsho dag/ mtha' yas par ni bzang po'i spyod spyad pa// de dag chos kyi dbyings rnams gang byas nas// thams cad
100a6(phal chen): chos kyi sprin las rab tu brjod// ning rnams ji ltar 'byung bar 'gyur ba dang // stobs bcu rnams kyang ji ltar 'thung 'gyur dang // sems can rgya mtsho ji ltar 'byung 'gyur ba// sems can rnams
100a7(phal chen): lasgra dbyangs gtong zhing ston// 'khor rnams yangs pa 'di dag thams cad kyang // kun tu bzang po khyod la mngon sum gnas// sangs rgyas kun gyis gnang bar gyur pa yi// chos kyi 'khor lo deri/ 
100a8(phal chen): khyod kyis bag/ shin rgyas mchen po'i mi pa rgyas pa la mam zhes bya bsas// kun tu ji 'i zhi dang / rnam par 'phrul b.rab tu grung zhes bya ste/ 
100b1(phal chen): gsum pa'o// / de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad la rnam par bltas/ sems can gyi kham
100b2(phal chen): rgya mtsho la rnam par bltas// chos kyi dbyings rgya mtsho la rnam par bltas/ sems can thams cad kyi las rgya mtsho la rnam par bltas/ sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa dang dbang po rgya mtsho la rnam
100b3(phal chen): par bltas/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos kyi rgya mtsho la rnam par bltas/ dus rgya mtsho la rnam par bltas/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yang dag par 'byung ba'i smon lam rgya mtsho la rnam par bltas/ 
100b4(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul pa rgya mtsho la rnam par bltas nas/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor yod pa thams cad la smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras
100b5(phal chen): ngag sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi kham sa zang 'dra zhing 'jig pa yongasu dag pa 'thung ba'i ye shes ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
100b6(phal chen): rnams kyi sems can thams cad kyi las 'thung ba rgya mtsho mkhyen pa ni bsam gyis mi khyabo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul rgya mtsho thams cad la rnam par gnas pa'i ya
100b7(phal chen): shes ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa rgya mtsho thams cad mtha' dang dpung med par bstan pa'i ye shes ni bsam gyis mi khyabo/ sa rgyas bcom ldan
100b8(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi sems can thams cad kyi las rgya mtsho rnam par dgod pa'i ye shes ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bsam pa dang dad pa dang / dbang po rgya mtsho la 'jug
101a1(phal chen): pa'i ye shes ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs kyi skad cig gcig la/ dus thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid thug su chud pa'i ye shes ni
101a2(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rnam par 'phral ba rgya mtsho yang dag par bstan pa'i ye shes ni bsam gyis mi khyabo// sangs rgyas bcom
101a3(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor ba'i ye shes ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rnam par dgod pa rab tu bstan pa rgya mtsho ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo// 
101a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi sku rab tu ba bstan pa yongs su dag pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi yon tan rgya mtsho mtha' dang dpung
101a5(phal chen): med pas rnam par snang ba ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgya/ sa bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po yong su dag pa ni bsam gyis mi khya'o// sangs rgyas bcom
101a6(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor yong su dag pa mtha' yas pa ni bsam gyis mi khya'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'od zer rgya mtsho kha dog sna tshogs kyi sprin rab tu 'gyed pa mdzad pa ni/ 
101a7(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi dpal rin po che'i 'od 'phro ba rgya mtsho rnam par rgyu ba ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
101a8(phal chen): kyi sangs rgyas kyi gsung dang dbyangs rgya mtsho rab tu 'grub pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi cho 'phrul rnam pa gsum yongasu bstan pas/ sems can rgya mtsho yongasu
101b1(phal chen): smin par mdzad pa dang / gdul ba mdzad pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gdul ba rgya mtsho thams cad la brtson padon yod pa ni bsam gyis
101b2(phal chen): mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi sa la rab tu bzhugs pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul la
101b3(phal chen): 'jug pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi byin gyi rlabs kyi mthu ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyi spyod
101b4(phal chen): yul rnam par rgyu ba ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas pa/ com ldan 'das rnams kyi stobs la thub pa med pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mi
101b5(phal chen): bsgrengs pa zil gyis mi non pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sang sa rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi ting 'ija na la tha mi dad par spyod pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas
101b6(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i rdzu 'phrul dang rnam par 'phral ba ni bsam gyis mi kha bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mnga' chen po'i ye shes rnam par dag pa ni bsam
101b7(phal chen): gyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos mi 'phrogs pa ni bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ de dag thams cad sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi rlabs
101b8(phal chen): kyis byin du rlabs pas/ sems can thams cad sangs rgyas kyi ye shes rgya mtsho la gzung ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan rgya mtsho la rab tu 'god pa dang / 
102a1(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad kyis rnam par brgyan pa dang / bskal pa rgya mtsho thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdung
102a2(phal chen): rjesu bsab pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du chos kyi rang bzhin gyi dkyil 'khor rab tu brjod pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi dad pa rgya mtsho tha dad pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu bstan pa
102a3(phal chen): dang / sems can thams cad kyi dbang po rgya mtsho la sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi tshul kun tu snang ba yang dag par bskyed pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa rgya mtsho'i sgrib pa'i ri thams cad rnam par
102a4(phal chen): gzhom pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi sems dang spyod pa rgya mtsho la 'byung ba'i lam rnam par sbyang ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho thams cad byang chub sems dpa'i smon
102a5(phal chen): lam rgya mtsho la rab tu dgod pa'i phyir yang dag par bstan par bya'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho rnams de bas kyang shin tu
102a6(phal chen): dga' bar bya ba dang / chos la dga' ba'i shugs thams cad rnam par 'phel bar bya ba dang / mos pa'i tshul yangs pa rgya mtsho yang dag par 'byung bar bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi rang bzhin dang / 
102a7(phal chen): snying po sgo kun dang ldan pa rnam par dag par bya ba dang / kun tu bzang po'i smon lam rgya mtsho la rab tu dgod par bya ba dang / ye shes kyi mig dus gsum gyi rjesu song ba yongasu sbyang ba dang / 'jig rten
102a8(phal chen): thams cad kun nas snang bar byed pa'i snying po shes rab chen po'i rgya mtsho rnam par 'phel bar bya ba dang / chos kyi 'khor lo thams cad yongasu gzung ba'i gzungs kyi stobs yang dag par bskyed pa dang / 
102b1(phal chen): snying po byang chub thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi yul thams cad rab tu brjod pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi tshul spang ba'i 'od chos kyi dbyings rgya chen po dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la ngag
102b2(phal chen): ba'i shugs rgya mtsho rnam par 'phel bar bya ba'i phyir/ de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smraso// yon tan rgya mtsho rnams kyi ye shes zab// mtha' dang dbung med des ni zhing rnams khyab// sems can
102b3(phal chen): bsam la sbyor ba ji bzhin snang // rnam par snang mdzad chos kyi 'khor lo'o// bsam gyis mi khyab rgya mtsho'i zhing yod pa// bskal pa rgya mtshor rgyal bas rnam sbyangs pas// sems can rgya mtsho
102b4(phal chen): yongs su sman bya'i phyir// sems can nang na rgyal ba rnam pa ra mdzes// sems can rgya mtsho 'byung ba bsam mi khyab// / sangs rgyas yul la 'jug pa shin tu zab// srid pa'i
102b5(phal chen): gnas can dad pa chung ba yis// sangs rgyas byang chub shes par mi nuso// gzhan du gang rnams shin tu sem sa brtan cing // dge ba'i bshes kyis yongasu bzung ba dang / 
102b6(phal chen): sangs rgyas kun gyi byin gyis brlabs pa dag/ sangs rgyas ye shes 'di la rab tu 'jug/ gang rnams sems dag g.yo med sgyu med cing // snying rje'i bsam can khong nas byams dga' dang / 
102b7(phal chen): dad pa che zhing rlabs chen de dag ni// 'di dag thos shing dga' ba thob par 'gyur// kun tu bzang po'i smon lam sa dag dang // chos dbyings na mkha'i dbyingasu khyab pa la// gnas shing spyod
102b8(phal chen): pa rab tu sus spyod pa// de dag rgyal ba'i spyod yul 'ang sheso// gang gis rgyal ba'i rnam 'phral 'di mthong ba'i// byang chub sems dpas thob bya legs par thob// gzhan gyi yul gyis
103a1(phal chen): shes par mi nus te// 'di ni kun tu bzang pos rtogs pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyis byin rlabs shing // 'gro ba mtha' dang dpung med 'di dag na// kun tu
103a2(phal chen): chos kyi 'khor lo rab 'khor ba// rnam par snang mdzad yul dang mthu yin no// bdag gi lus su zhing rnams thams cad kyang // rab tu zhugs shing de zhugs zhing rnams kun// de dag spu rtse kun
103a3(phal chen): tu blta bar gyis// rgyal ba'i spyod yul shin tu bshad par bya// kun tu bzang po'i smon lam spyod pa rnams// mtha' dang dpung med mngon par sgrub pa dang // kun tu mig gi yul dang lus ldan
103a4(phal chen): pa// de dag mgon po'i spyod yul 'di nyan to// kye rgyal po'i sras dag bcu po 'di dag ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho shi ngan tu bstan pa ste// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa
103a5(phal chen): dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba rnams kyis gsung so// gsung ngo // gsung bar 'gyuraro// bcu gang zhe na/ 'di/ lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams yongs su 'byung ba'i tshogs kyi rgyu
103a6(phal chen): rkyen shin tu bstan pa dang / 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gnas pa shin tu bstan pa dang / 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i dbyibs dang rnam pa shin tu bstan pa dang / 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi
103a7(phal chen): khams rgya mtsho'i lhun shin tu bstan pa dang / 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rgyan shin tu bstan pa dang / 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho yongasasu dag par bya ba'i tshul shin tu bstan pa dang / 
103a8(phal chen): 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag tu sangs rgyas 'byung ba shin tu bstan pa dang / 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i bskal pa'i byin gyi rlabs shin tu bstan pa dang / 'di lta ste/ bskal pa/ 
103b1(phal chen): mtha' yas pa'i rgyud rgya mtsho shin tu bstan pa rang 'i/ sde 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho tha mi dad pa shin tu bstan pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho bcu po 'di dag la sogs pa
103b2(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho shin tu bstan pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba rnams kyis gsung so// 
103b3(phal chen): gsung// gsung bar 'gyuraro// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad ni rgyu dang rkyen la dmigs pa'i sgo// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba sring phrag
103b4(phal chen): bcus byung ngo // 'byung ngo // 'byung bar 'gyuraro// bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis rlabs dang chos nyid rab tu thob pa dang / sems can rnams
103b5(phal chen): kyi las kyi tshogs dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cacan mkhyen pa nyid du yang dag par sgrub pa'i chos nyid dang / sem sa can rnams kyis kyang byang chub sems dpa' dag dang / 
103b6(phal chen): bsod nams kyi rtsa ba skal pa 'thun pa bsags pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi zhing yongs dag pa'i smon lam gyi khyad par dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pas rnam par bsgrubs
103b7(phal chen): pa'i smon lam gyis mngon par bsgrubs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mos pa'i dbang rnam par dag pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i jig rten las 'das po dang / 
103b8(phal chen): rgyu 'thun pas mngon par 'tshang rgya zhing sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa khyu mchog gi mthung byung ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po rnams kyi smon lam gyis smon par 'phrul bi'o sgo'o// 
104a1(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras pa// de chub rkyen la rigs pa'i sgobacu po di dag la sogs brgyad da rkyen la dmigs pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mdo'i rdul shin tu phra basbed kyis 'chi
104a2(phal chen): 'thung ngo // 'thung bar 'gyuraro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byung ba shin tu bstan pa 'di nyid gsal bar brjod pa'i phyir/ 
104a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis/ de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smras// sangs rgyas ye shes yul ni bsam yas pas// bin rlabs rnam 'phral de dag 'di lta bu// zhing rnams
104a4(phal chen): rgya mtsho bstan pa mtha' dbud med// rnam par snang mdzad chos kyis yongasu sbyangs// byang chub sems dpa' kun gyi ba sam pa bzhin// smon lam rgya mtsho bas ma yas rnam sbyangs
104a5(phal chen): shing // sems can las rnams rgya mtsho bsam yas pas// phyogs kun zhing rnams rgya mtsho thams cad 'byung // byang chub sems dpa' kun gyi rnam 'phrul dang // thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la
104a6(phal chen): 'jug pa'i sgos// smon lam rgya mtsho thams cad mngon bsgrubs shing // na mkha'i dbyings la 'byam klas zhing 'byung // spyod pa rgya mtsho mtha' dang dpung med rnams// spyod cing tshad med bad gshegs yul
104a7(phal chen): la 'jug/ phyogs kyi zhing rnams rgya mtsho kun sbyong zhing // bskal pa mtha' yas zhing rnams re re spyod// sems can bsam dbyings bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i// las kyis zhing rnams rgya mtsho thams cad thub
104b1(phal chen): nyon mongs las kyis de dag nyon mongs bcas/ mos dang bsam pas rnam pa sna tshogs gzugs// zhing rnams rgya mtsho rnam dag rgyan can rnams// rin chen rgyus byung sna tshogs dri med pa// rang ngargya
104b2(phal chen): mtshe rnam par spel ba'i phyir// rgyal sras rnams ni phyogs bcur zhing rnams sbyong // chos dbyings rdul gyi khongasu rgyal sras rnams// kun tu bzang po'i spyad pa spyod pa dag/ rdul gyi khongasu mtha' yas ning
104b3(phal chen): ston te// rnam dag mkha' bzhin mtha' dang dpung yang med// namakha'i dbyings 'dra'i rnam 'phrul 'di 'dra ste// snying po byang chub rgyal ba'i zhabs drung na// pad+mo'i bstan 'khod kha dog mtha' yas kun/ 
104b4(phal chen): de dag zhing bcas lus kyi nang na 'khod// skad cig sems kyis dus gsum byung ba yi// zhing 'byung tshul dang 'jug pa kun kyang ston// sangs rgyas rnams kyis dus gsum zhing stan pa/ 
104b5(phal chen): rnam par snang mdzad rgya mtsho'i zhing mi zad// tshul gyi khang pa ra mtha' yas sna tshogs pas// rdul rnams kun la mtha'ayas rgyan gyi rnams// sangs rgyas skad cig gcig lu'in
104b6(phal chen): gyis rlob// rgyal gyi rnam pa tshal kun rab tu mkhan// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de la gnas pa shin tu bstan pa ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho re re zhing yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu
104b7(phal chen): pra bsred de// 'di ltar 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni// rgyan thams cad kyi rgya mtsho kun la rab tu gnaso// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni na mkha'i dbyings kyi gnas la rab tu gnaso/ 
104b8(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che thams cad kyi 'od zer gyi rgya mtsho la rab tu gnaso// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho la rab tu
105a1(phal chen): gnaso// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog gi mdog la rab tu gnaso// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni sangs rgyas thams cad
105a2(phal chen): dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor la rab tu gan so// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni sgyu ma lta bu'i las kyis byung ba/ lha ma yin dang mthu bo che lta bu'i lag na rdo rje rgya mtsho la rab tu gnaso// 'jig rten gyi khams
105a3(phal chen): rgya mtsho la la ni 'jig rten gyi dbang po thams cad kyi lus kyi gzugs brnyan rgya mtsho la rab tu gnaso// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi lus rgya mtsho la rab tu
105a4(phal chen): gnaso// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i smon lam gyis byung ba'i rgyan rnam pa thams cad dang ldan pa'i rgya mtsho la rab tu gnas te/ de dag la sogs
105a5(phal chen): pa 'jig rten gyi khams rab tu gnas pa shin tu bstan pa ni/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho re re zhing yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed do// de nas byang chub
105a6(phal chen): sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho rab tu gnas pa shin tu bstan pa'i don 'di nyid yongasu bstan pa'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi mthus// de'i tshe tshigasu bcad pa 'di dag smraso// 
105a7(phal chen): kun kyang zhing rnams rgya mtsho 'di dag rin chen rang bzhin dri med pa// rnam dag sna tshogs nor bu kun 'bar 'od zer rgya mtsho'i 'od ldan ltos// 'di dag rgyal ba'i byin rlab rgyu yis dbyings legs
105a8(phal chen): 'khor bar rnam par snang // de dag gis ni phyogs bcu'i na mkha'i dbyings rnams gzhi kun rab tu khyab// zhing rnams rgya mtsho dri med 'ongs nan mkha'i dbyings la gnas// snang ba'i snying po 'od
105b1(phal chen): san nor bu'i rgya mtsho ga la legs par gnas// 'gro ba de dbus rgyal ba 'khor la chos kyi 'khor lo bzang po skor// 'di ni sangs rgyas yul yin sems can rgya chen shin tu mgu byed pa'o// la la
105b2(phal chen): me tog sgron ma kun tu rgyas pa'i mu tig nor bus brgyan// 'od zer dra ba'i kun nas sprin 'bar spos 'phro sprin gyi 'od can te// zhing mang mtha' dang dpung med rgya chen pad+mo'i rgya mtsho dag la gnas/ 
105b3(phal chen): sangs rgyas rnams kyis rab brgyan zhing rnams 'bam klas kun kyang rab tu mdzes// zhing rnams rgya mtsho dkyil 'khor dbyings rnams la la sangs rgyas byin la gnas// yangs shing rin chen mang
105b4(phal chen): ldan rgya che de dag byang chub sems dpas gang // lag na rdo rje rgya mtsho mang tshogs lha dbang lus la de bzhin gnas// de na bcom ldan rnam par snang ba mdzad kyi 'khor lo rtag tu 'khor
105b5(phal chen): rer bu'i shing dang spos kyi 'phro'i sprin rnams mnyam pa'i daphyi/ ngas la gnas// chu'i phung po dag dang rdo rje rgya mtsho brtan la'ang de bzhin gnas// la la gos dang brag dang rgyal mtsha
105b6(phal chen): me tog sna tshogs rgya mtsho dag la gnas// kun na'ang rnam 'phrul 'di dag rgya chen rnam par snang mdzad ston pa mdzad// zhing rnams ring dang thung dang glong gi gzugs dang rnam pa sna tshogs te// sna
105b7(phal chen): tshegs rgyan can snying po dri ma bral ba yongs dag dri med snang // rnam pa sna tshogs de dag smon lam rgya mtsho'i dbyings la rab tu gnas// sangs rgyas sprin gyis kun nas yog par rtag tu na mkha'i
105b8(phal chen): dbyings la gnas// zhing rnams rgya mtsho 'bam klas la la spyi'u tshugs yod dang med la gnas// byang chub sems dpa'i co gzhi chen 'khor los bzung bas dag par gnas// de nas sangs rgyas
106a1(phal chen): rnam 'phrul rgya chen thams cad kun nas rab tu snang rin chen sangs rgyas gsung rnams kun tu gtong ldan las kyis de dag sprul// chos kyi dbyings mnyam zhing rnams 'ab
106a2(phal chen): klas mig yor sgyu ma dang yang 'dra// mig 'phrul rnam phye rnam dag dri med sems kyis shin tu bskyed pa ste// nam mkha'i dbyings rnams sna tshogs rgyan gyi snying po gnas 'gyur 'di la snang // las kyi
106a3(phal chen): yul ni bsam gyis mi khyab 'di dag bde bar gshegs pas bstan// skad cig sems kyis zhing rnams 'byam klas 'gro ba kun dang mnyam pa'i rnams// zhing rdul kun la kun tu bzang po rtag par
106a4(phal chen): rab tu sgrub byed cing // de na bskal pa rgya mtshor 'gro ba smin pa rub phyir spyad pa spyod// chos dbyings rgyas par bkang ste de dag kun tu rnam 'phrul rgya che ston// rdul rnams kun na chos
106a5(phal chen): dbyings yangs pa'i zhing rnams rgya mtsho kun kyang gnas// sangs rgyas sprin gyis byin gyis brlabs pas kun kyang yog cing yongasu rgyas// ji ltar rdul phran gcig la rnam sprul pa
106a6(phal chen): bzhin 'gro ba kun na'o// rnam par snang ba'i sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul rgya chen rab tu ston pa mdzad// zhing rnams 'byam klas thams cad mig yor lta bu sgyu ma smig rgyu 'dra// snang ba med cing 'byung
106a7(phal chen): med phyogs bcu dag na 'gro dang 'ong ba med// mkha' la gnas pa de dag rtag par byung zhing 'jig par de bzhin 'gyur// shin tu yangs pa de dag smon lam rnam sbyangs las kyis yongasu bzung / 
106a8(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho rnams kyi dbyings ni rnam pa sna tshogs te/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni kun nas zlum po'o// 'jig rten gyi khams
106b1(phal chen): rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni kun nas gru bzhi'o// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni na mkha'i rnam pa du mar rnam par phye ba'o// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa
106b2(phal chen): la la ni kun nas 'khyil pa'i dbyibs su 'dug go// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni 'od 'phro ba'i ri'i dbyibs su 'dug go// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la
106b3(phal chen): ni shing sna tshogs kyi lhun gyi dbyibs su 'dug go// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni me tog sna tshogs kyi dbyibasu 'dug go// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'bum klas pa la
106b4(phal chen): la ni khyim sna tshogs kyi dbyibasu 'dug go// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni sems can sna chog ras kyi lus kyi dbyings su 'dug go// 'jig rten gyi khams
106b5(phal chen): rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa la la ni mtshan sna tshogs kyi dbyibasu 'dug ste// de dag la sogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams kyi dbyibs shin tu bstan pa ni/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya
106b6(phal chen): mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed do// de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i dbyibs kyi tshul rgya mtsho 'di nyid yongasu bstan pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas
106b7(phal chen): kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa'adi dag smraso// rnam pa sna tshogs rgya mtsho'i zhing la ltos// rnam bye sna tshogs mtha' yas dbang
106b8(phal chen): su gnas// dbyibs kyis rnam par phye ba sna tshogs te// phyogs rnams kun na zhing rnams rgya mtsho snang // la la zlum po la la zur gsum ste// de dag la la phyogs na gru bzhir gnas/ 
107a1(phal chen): nor bu pad+mo 'khor lo yan lag brgyad// kun kyang las rnams mchos rnam par bris// rdul med 'od kyi dbyibs dang tshul 'dzin cing // gser las grub pa
107a2(phal chen): rnam bye sna tshogs te// sgo mang mtha' yas pa nas rgyu zhing 'jug/ las rnams rgya mtsho bsam pa dag pas gnas// zhing rnams rgya mtsho sna tshogs snying po can// nam mkha' 'di la ji ltar sprin
107a3(phal chen): gnas bzhin// de dag rin chen mang gzhi rnam par phye// de dag kun na sangs rgyas rnam par mdzes// zhing rnams 'di kun sems kyis rnam par brtags// sna tshogs rgyan dang snang bas kun na
107a4(phal chen): gnas// rnam par 'phrul pa gzhan dang gzhan dag gis// zhing rnams rgya mtsho sangs rgyas ston pa mdzad// bde dang sdug bsngal myong bar gyur pa ni// rnam par ngag dang nyon mongs
107a5(phal chen): tshul bzhin te// chos nyid 'di ni rtag tu yod pa yin// de lta/ 'a las rnams rgya mtsho bsam mi khyab// skra gcig rtse la da sam gyis mi khyab zhing // thams cad rdul snyed sna tshogs
107a6(phal chen): dbyibs su gnas// kun na sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad bzhugs// 'khor rnams rgya mtsho chos rnams rab tu ston// rdul gcig rtse la phra dang yangs pa'i rnams// thams cad rdul snyed kha
107a7(phal chen): dog dbyibs rnams kun kyang rnam par brtags// de dag kun na rgyal ba'i 'khor lo 'khor// rdul rnams kun la rab tu zhing bstan pa// de dag smon lam rnam par sprul pa yin// na mkha'i
107a8(phal chen): dbyingasu las kyi sprul pa ni// sna tshogs sems dang bsam pa rnam par brtags// sems can kun mnyam rdul rnams thams cad la// sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul pa sprul pa dag/ rnam
107a9(phal chen): bar snang mdzad chos nying de yin te// rdul phran kun la zhing rnams shin tu gnas// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i lhun ngag ni gzhan dang gzhan du shes par bya ste// 'di ltar 'jig rtenas
107b1(phal chen): gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che'i rgyan thams cad kyi lhun can no// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni/ rin po che gcig las rnam pa sna tshogs su bkong pa'i rgyan gyi lhun can
107b2(phal chen): no// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che'i rgyan thams cad kyi 'od zer gyi lhan can no// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni 'od kha dog sna tshogs kyi lhun can no// 
107b3(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rgyan thams cad kyi mdog gi lhun san mo// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rdo rje'i gzhi mi shigs pa'i lhun can no// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni
107b4(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi rdzu 'phrul dang / byin gyi brlabs kyi lhun can no// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che'i mtsha na nyid kyi lhun tsano// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni sa
107b5(phal chen): rgyas kyis sprul pa'i lhun can no// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni nyi ma'i nor bu'i dkyil 'khor gyi lhun can no// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che shin
107b6(phal chen): tu phra ba 'dzin pa'i lhun can no// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni snang ba'i lhun cano// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog 'od 'phro ba'i rnam pa'i lhan
107b7(phal chen): can no// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni dri dang kha dog sna tshogs kyi spos kyi lhun can no// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che thams cad kyi me tog gi cod pan gyi ldan can
107b8(phal chen): no// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che thams cad kyi 'od kyi lhun can no// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rgyan thams cad shin tu bstan pa'i lhun can no// 'jig rten
108a1(phal chen): gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni sems kyi rnam par rtog pa skad cig gis dmigs pa thams cad yongasu bstan pa'i lhun can no// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni byang chub
108a2(phal chen): sems dpa'i lus kyi rin po che'i dbyings kyi lhun can no// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni rin po che thams cad kyi me tog gi ze bi'i lhun can no// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho la la ni sangs
108a3(phal chen): rgyas thams cad kyi gsung dbyangs rnam par rimigs pa'i lhun can no// de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos// yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i lhun shin tu bstan pa rgya mtsho 'ang
108a4(phal chen): la rab tu gzung bar bya ba'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe ni gsu bcad pa 'di dag smras// zhing rnams rgya mtsho la la ni/ 
108a5(phal chen): rin chen rang bzhin kun nas gnas// rdo rje bzhin du mi shigs sra// rin chen pad+mo rnams la gnas// la la 'od zla/ ra rang bzhin te// dag cing gzung med 'od zer 'thung // rgyan rnam
108a6(phal chen): kun gyi 'od zer gyis// sna tshogs mkha' bzhin dri ma med// la la 'od kyi rang bzhin te// dag cing 'od gsal zer la gnas// 'od kyi sprin can sna tshogs 'od // byang chub sems dpa' rnams
108a7(phal chen): kyi gnas// zhing rnams rgya mtsho la la ni// mig yor lta bur gnas pa ste// brjod du med cing gzung du med// smon lam dbang gis rab tu byung // la la nor bu mu tig rgyu// snying po thams cad
108a8(phal chen): 'bar// mu tig 'khor lo'i gni dag pa// byang chub sems dpas yongasu gang // rin chen 'od 'phro byung ba'i zhing // 'od 'phro'i sprin gyis mngon khebs shing // rin chen thams cad sna tshogs ldan/ 
108b1(phal chen): thams cad las kyis sprul pa yin// la la mtshan las byung ba ste// gzhi kun mtshan gyis kun tu bris// cod pan rnam pa sna tshogs bkod// sangs rgyas kun gyis mngon par sprul// rgya
108b2(phal chen): mtsho'i sems las byung ba yi// zhing rnams mos pa nyid la gnas// yul na mi gnas sgyu ma gzhin// yongasu rtog pas yang dag bskyed// sangs rgyas sku'i 'od zer gyi// nor bus sna tshogs kun
108b3(phal chen): tu gnas// sangs rgyas sprin rnams rnam par snang // sangs rgyas kun gyis rab tu sprul// la la kun tu bzang po yis// zhing rnams rgya mtsho shin tu sprul// na mkha'i rgyan rnams thams cad dang / 
108b4(phal chen): smon lam rnams kyis rnam par bris// kye rgyal ba'i sras drag/ de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rgyan shin tu ba snyan pa ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed
108b5(phal chen): du shes par bya ste/ 'di ltar dmigs pa rnam pa sna tshogs thams cad kyi sprin rab tu 'phros pa'i rgyan dang / 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi yon tan gyi 'kho
108b6(phal chen): lo rje su brjod cing rab tu 'byung ba'i rgyan dang / 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gtogs pa'i sems can rnams kyi las rnam par smin pa rgya mtsho las rab tu byung ba'i rgyan dpa'i
108b7(phal chen): ste/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi smon lam rgya mtsho'i glong yongasu ston pa'i rgyan dang / 'di lta ste/ dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gzugs brnyan sna tshogs rnam par dmigs pa'i
108b8(phal chen): rgyan dang / 'di lta ste/ sems kyi skad cig la bskal pa mtha' yas par rnam par 'phrul pa'i yul yongasu ston pa'i rgyan dang / 'di lta ste/ rgyan gyi dmigs pa thams cad las sangs rgyas kyi sku ba
109a1(phal chen): tu 'byung ba'i rgyan dang / 'di lta ste/ rin po che dang / spos thams cad kyi sprin rab tu 'byung ba'i rgyun dang / 'di lta ste/ snying po byang chub kyi rgyan dang / 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi rnam par
109a2(phal chen): ston pa'i rgyan dang / 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i smon lam dang / spyod pa yongasu ston pa'i rgyan dag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de dag la sogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i
109a3(phal chen): rgyan shin tu bstan pa ni/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed do// de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rgyan shin tu bstan pa 'di nyid yongs
109a4(phal chen): su bstan pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigasu bcad pa 'di dag smraso// zhing rnams rgya mtsho'i rgya che mtha' yas te// rnam dag
109a5(phal chen): las kyi rnam pa sna tshogs gnas// phyogs bcu'i zhing rnam sa rgya mtsho rnams kun kyang // sna tshogs rgyan can yang / sa par kun nas gnas/ kha dog sna tshogs yangs pa'i zhi dge
109a6(phal chen): rnams// rgya mtsho rtag par phyogs rnams kun tu 'byung // rgyan dang rin chen 'od 'phro sna tshogs sprin// sgra 'byin zhing gi dbyings rnams khebs par byed// byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan rgya mtsho
109a7(phal chen): rnams// de dag kun kyang rgya mtsho'i zhing na grag/ sna tshogs rgyan dang smon lam sprin gyi rnams// de dag zhing mang rgya mtshor sgra yang 'byin// 'gro ba'i las rnams rgya mtsho yangs pa dag/ rgyan gyi sprin
109a8(phal chen): rnams kun nas sgrar 'byin te// sems can de dag rnam smin ji 'dra ba// sangs rgyas byin gyis kun nas sgra yang sgrog/ dus gsum 'byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa yi// rnam 'phrul zhing rnams
109b1(phal chen): rgya mtsho kun na snang // dmigs pa re re la yang sangs rgyas kun// de 'dra'i zhing mang rgya mtsho'i rgyan la ltos// 'das pa'i bskal pa de bzhin ma 'ongs dang // phyogs bcu'i nga ltar byung brji
109b2(phal chen): sbed pa'i// bskal pa de dag rgyan mang yangs pa yang // zhing rnams rgya mtsho re re dag na snang // dmigs pa kun la sangs rgyas sprin gyi rnams// 'gro dang mnyam pas 'jig rten kun tu 'gangs/ 
109b3(phal chen): rnam par 'phrul zhing sems can rnam par 'dul// 'di ni zhing rnams rgya mtsho'i rnam thar to// spos 'od sprin dang de bzhin me tog klong // rgyan rnams sna tshogs thams cad kun nas kyang / 
109b4(phal chen): rtag par kun tu khyab par rab tu 'byung // 'di ni zhing rnam sa rgya mtsho'i rnam thar to// phyogs bcu kun gyi snying po bya ngang chub rnams// sna tshogs rgyan canas ma lus par/ 
109b5(phal chen): thams cad rgya mtsho'i zhing 'di dbyings dag na// nam kha'i sprin bzhin rnam par ston pa snang // rgyal sras kun tu bzang po thams cad kyi// zhing rnams mtha'
109b6(phal chen): yas 'bum klas rgyan gyi rnams// 'gro ba'i grangs sreng bskal pa rgya mtshor rnam sbyangs pa// zhing rnams rgya mtsho kun nas rab tu snang // kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'jig rten gyi
109b7(phal chen): khams rgya mtsho yongasu dag par bya ba'i tshul rgya mtsho ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du shes par bya ste/ 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen
109b8(phal chen): thams cad la brtan pa'i dge ba'i rtsa bas skal ba mnyam pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings kyi bsod nams rgya chen po'i sngon rnam par 'phel bar bya ba dang / byang chub sems
110a1(phal chen): dpa' rnams kyi mos pa'i dkyil 'khor rgya chen po rnam par dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa' thams cad rab tu brtan pa'i yul la rnam par
110a2(phal chen): spyod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rgya mtsho thams cad yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / yongs su sbyang ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i sa thams
110a3(phal chen): cad kyi dbyings la rab tu dgod cing bzung ba'i rnam par spyod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa dang / 'byung ba rgya mtsho la rnam par spyod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi smon lam rgya mtsho tham
110a4(phal chen): cad mngon par bsgrub pa rnam par dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rgya mtsho thams cad mngon par bsgrub pa rnam par dag pa la rab tu 'jug pa dang / 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa'
110a5(phal chen): rnams kyi stobs kyi tshul yang dag par bsgrubs pa rnam par/ dag pa dang / de dag la sogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya ma/ tshe yongs su dag par bya ba'i tshul rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams
110a6(phal chen): rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du shes par bya'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho yong su dag par bya ba'i tshul rgya mtsho 'di nyid rnam par bstan pa'i
110a7(phal chen): phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigasu bcad pa 'di dag smras// zhing rnams rgya mtsho thams cad sna tshogs rgyan// smon lam tshul rnams rgya mtsha
110a8(phal chen): kun gyis byung // kha dog mtha' yas las kyi rgya mtshos dag / zhing rnams rgya mtsho rtag tu 'od mang 'gyed// sngan chad dge ba'i bshes gnyen bsnyen bkur cing // skal ba mnyam pa'i las dge yongs spya
110b1(phal chen): te/ snying rje byams pas 'gro yangs kun bkang zhing // zhing rnams rgya mtsho yangs pa 'di kun sbyangs// chos sgo kun tu ting 'dzin sa kun gyis// sangs rgyas yon tan rgya mtsho yongs sbyangs te// bsam gtan tshul
110b2(phal chen): dang rnam thar sa sbyang zhing // zhing rnams rgya mtsho sna tshogs yangs pa byung // mos pa'i dkyil 'khor mtha' yas stobs bskyed cing // rgyal ba'i mnyam nyid ma nor rtogs byas nas// bzod pa rgya mtsho'i tshul rnams
110b3(phal chen): yongs sbyangs shing // rnam dag kha dog mtha' yas ning rnams byung // bsod nams sprin ni na mkha' mnyam bskyed cing // 'gro ba kun phan pade don spyod spyad de// bsod nams rgya mtsho sems can kun bstan pa/ 
110b4(phal chen): 'jig rjer khams rnams rgya mtsho kun kyang 'byung // zhing rnam sa rgya mtsho'iri rdul skad tshad med pa'i// pha rol phyin pa ma lus kun sbyangs te// smon lam mthar phyin mi zang sems bas
110b5(phal chen): pas// dri mang rgya mtsho'i zhing rnams yangs pa 'byung // 'thung ba'i spyod pa gang yod tshang med dang // chos rnams thams cad yang sa pa yongs sbyangs te// sna tshogs thabs sgos sems can sbya
110b6(phal chen): pas na// 'di 'dra'i yid 'ongs rgya mtsho'i zhing rnams 'byung // rgyan rnams kun gyi tshul dang sa sbyangs shing // rgyal ba'i yon tan rgya mtsho kun zhugs nas// 'gro ba kun gyi sdug bsngal mtsho skams pas// nang
110b7(phal chen): bi mtsho yangs 'di kun dag par 'gyur// stobs rnams rgya mtsho gzhal med yongs sbyangs shing // 'gro ba 'di 'dra tshad med rnam sbyangs te// sangs rgyas rgya mtsho yangs kun bsnyen bkur bas// zhing rnams rgya
110b8(phal chen): mtsho rnam mang rnam par dag/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho re rer sangs rgyas 'byung ba'i tshul rgya mtsho ni// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du shes par
111a1(phal chen): ba ste/ 'di ltar sangs rgyas 'thung ba la la ni sku chung ngur kun tu ston to// 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas 'byung ba la la ni chos kyi dbyings thams cad gzugs kyi skus gang bar ston to// 
111a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas 'byung ba la la ni sku tshe tshang mi ring ngo // sangs rgyas 'byung ba la la ni sku tshe'i tshad ring ngo // sangs rgyas 'byung ba la la ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing cig yong su dag par byin gyis rlob bo// sangs
111a3(phal chen): rgyas 'byung ba la la ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad yong su dag par byin gyis rlob bo// sangs rgyas 'byung ba la la ni tshul gcig gis bstan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo byin gyis rlob bo// sangs rgyas
111a4(phal chen): 'byung ba la la ni tshul bsam gyis mi khyab par bstan pa'i chos kyi 'a khor lo byin gyis rlob bo// sangs rgyas 'byung ba la la ni sems can gyi khams nyung ngu rnam par gdul ba biran gyis rlob bo// sangs rgyas
111a5(phal chen): 'byung ba la la ni sems can rgya mtsho mtha' yas pa rnam par gdu la ba byin gyis rlob ste/ de dag la sogs pa 'jig rten gyi kham sa rgya mtsho re rer sangs rgyas 'byung ba'i tshul rgya mtsho 'jig
111a6(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du shes par bya'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yang sangs rgyas 'byung ba'i tshul rgya mtsho'i phyogs 'di nyid yongasu bstan pa'i phyir/ 
111a7(phal chen): rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te// de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smraso// rgyal ba 'byung ba thabs rnams sna tshogs kyi// sgo nas zhing rnams rgya mtshor rab tu 'byung // de dag
111a8(phal chen): sems can bsam pa ji bzhin mkhyen// sangs rgyas thabs kyi sgo mang rgya mtsho'o// sangs rgyas chos sku bsam gyis mi khyab ste// mig yor ma yin mtshan nyid med pa'i gzugs// gzugs kyi khang
111b1(phal chen): par 'gro ba 'di dag tu// sems can bsam pa'i phyogs bzhin ston la ltos// sku che thung bsas rnam par ston// la la bskal pa bsam yas byin gyis rlob// chos kyi sku ni phyogs rnams kun gyi sgo// rab
111b2(phal chen): mdzes par 'gro nang 'di na bzhugs// la la zhing rnams rgya mtsho bas ma yas dag/ skyong zhing 'bam klas phyogs bcu kun na yang // la la zhing gcig rnam par sbyong bar mdzad// smon lam ma lus kun kya
111b3(phal chen): tshul gcig go// la la bsam gyis mi khab theg pa'i rgyan// sems can yid bzhin sangs rgyas ston pa mdzad// la la theg pa gcig kyang rab ston te// rgyal ba'i thabs ni gcig kyang mtha' ya so// rang
111b4(phal chen): nga la la byang chub sangs rgyas nas// sems can mi mngal/ ma la gzhog pa mdzad// la la skad cig gcig gis sems can rnams// rgya mtsho bsam yas byang chub don tu 'dul/ 
111b5(phal chen): la spu'i sgonas bsam yas pa'i// sangs rgyas sprul pa'i sprin rnams rab tu 'gyeng // 'gro ba kun tu de dag mngon bkang zhing / thabs kyi sgo nas sems can 'dul ba mdzad// la las/ 
111b6(phal chen): rgyas gsung gis kun bkang zhing // zhing du sems can yid bzhin rab tu sgrog/ bsam yas bskal par de dag gsung sgeg cing // sems can rgya mtsho mtha' yas rnam par 'dul// la la zhing rgyan bsal
111b7(phal chen): gyis mi khab ste// 'khor rnams yongs dag kun nas 'khod bcas pas// zhing mang rgya mtsho phyog su gdubyas shing // sangs rgyas mkha' la sprin ltar khyab par bzhugs// de ltar sangs rgyas/ 
111b8(phal chen): ni bsam mi khyab/ zhing rnams rgya mtsho kunang rgyas bkang zhing // 'gro bkun la sangs rgyas mngon sum ste// sna tshogs rgyan mang du ma'i tshul dang ldan// kyai rgyal ba'i sras dag de la 'jig rten gyi rnams
112a1(phal chen): rgya mtsho'i bskal pa'i byin gyis brlabs kyi tshul shin tu bstan pa ni// 'jig can gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du shes par ba ste/ 'di ltar zhing rgya ma
112a2(phal chen): la ni bskal pa grangs med par byin gyis brlabs pa'o// zhing rgya mtsho la la ni bskal pa tshad med par byin gyis brlabs pa'o// zhing rgya mtsho la la ni bskal pa dpag tu med par byin gyis brlabs pa'o// zhing
112a3(phal chen): rgya mtsho la la ni bskal pa bsam gyis mi khyab par byin gyis brlabs pa'o// zhing rgya mtsho la la ni bskal pa mtshungs pa med par byin gyis brlabs po'o// zhing rgya mtsho la la ni bskal pa kun nas mtha'
112a4(phal chen): yas par byin gyis rlabs pa'o// zhing rgya mtsho la la ni bskal pa kun nas mu med par byin gyis brlabs pa'o// zhing rgya mtsho la la ni bskal pa gzhal du med par byin gyis brlabs pa'o// zhing
112a5(phal chen): rgya mtsho la la ni bskal pa brjod du med par byin gyis brlabs pa ste/ de dag la sogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i bskal pa'i byin gyis brlabs kyis tshul shin tu bstan pa rgya
112a6(phal chen): mtsho ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba skang ngo // de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i bskal pa'i byin gyis rlabs kyi tshul shin tu bstan pa
112a7(phal chen): 'di nyid yongasu bstan pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smras// 'jig rten rgya mtsho bskal pa tha dad // sna tshogs
112a8(phal chen): tshul 'jug rgyan rnams gzhan dang gzhan// phyogs bcu'i zhing rnams rgya mtsho kun na snang // bskal pa'i tshul ni rgya mtsho grangs kyang med// bskal pa mi mthun 'gro ba kun dang mnyam// phyogs
112b1(phal chen): dbyings 'jig rten rgya mtsho'i khams na snang // bskal pa mtha' yas la la ring dang thung // bskal pa sna tshogs rgyal ba'i sgras kyang bsgrags// rgya mtsho'i zhing rnams 'di dag phyogs dbyings sdang // byin rlabs
112b2(phal chen): bskal pa zhing rdul sbed dang ldan// la la gzhan rnams bskal pa gcig gis 'jug/ la la bskal grangs smon lam dums byung // bskal pa la la dri med la la nyon mongs can// la la rnam dag la la nyon
112b3(phal chen): mongs rnam par gnas// bskal pa'i ming ni smon lam rgya mtsho'i tshul gyis byung // sems can 'du shes rnam pas tha dad tshul la 'jug/ bskal pa zhing gi rdul snyed sngan chad spyod spyad pas// 'jig rten la/ 
112b4(phal chen): rnams rgya mtsho shin tu yangs shing dag/ de dag kun nas sang sa rgyas yul rgyun chad kyang med// 'di dag rgya chen bskal pa 'i 'jig rten rgya mtsho'i khams// bskal pa'i 'od dang 'od
112b5(phal chen): zer rin chen ming sna tshogs// bcom ldan 'das dang 'od man/ ma 'od 'phro'i mig snang ba// snang dang dri med bzang po bskal pa'i ming la 'jug/ bskal pa 'di dag rnam dag bas
112b6(phal chen): pa kun las byung // dri med bskal pa la lar sangs rgyas gcig skye'o// bskal pa la lar mi'i gtso bo mtha' yas 'thung // bskal pa'i tshul rnams thams cad sa tshul zad mi shes// smon lam
112b7(phal chen): stobs mthus bskal pa sna tshogs 'jug par 'gyur// bskal pa la la mtha' yas rnams kyang bskal pa gcig tu 'dus// bskal pa la la gcig kyang bskal pa bye ba'i mthu// bskal pa rgya
112b8(phal chen): mtsho kun kyang sna tshogs sgo nas 'jug/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten khams kyi nang nas sgra yang 'byin// bskal pa la lar bskal pa kun gyi rgyan kyang 'byung // ming gi rgyan rnams rnam par
113a1(phal chen): dag pa'ang de la yod// bskal pa la la sangs rgyas rdzu 'phrul mthu yis byung // bskal pa'i tshul rnams kun gyi 'di ni rgyan yangs yin// zhing dang bskal pa rgya mtsho du na
113a2(phal chen): gcig gis dag/ zhing gi rdul rnams kun kyang tshad med gzhal du med// skad cig yud tsam nyi ma'i grangs kyi bskal par 'gyur// 'di dag thams cad sems can 'du shes rnam par 'byung // kye rgyal ba'i sras dag
113a3(phal chen): de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag bskal pas mtha' yas pa'i rgyud kyi tshul rgya mtsho ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba skad du shes par bya ste/ 'di ltar chos nyid rab tu thob pas 'jig
113a4(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag bskal pas 'jig cing 'du ba la rab tu 'jug par gnas pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtshor gto/ gus pa'i sems can rnams kyi nyon mongs pas bskal pa mtha'
113a5(phal chen): yas pa kun nas gnas pa dang / 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi/ khams rgya mtshor gtogs pa'i sems can rnams kyi bsod/ nams rgya mtsho rgya chen po bsags pa/ rnam par dag pas 'jig
113a6(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtsho kun nas nyon mongs la rnam par dag par gnas pa dang / 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' mos pa sna tshogs kyis spyod pa rnams skye bas 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho rnam par dag la
113a7(phal chen): kun nas nyon mongs par gnas pa dang / 'di lta ste/ sems can rgya mtsho rgya chen po byang chub kyi sems la gnas pas 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho shin tu dag par gnas pa dang / 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems
113a8(phal chen): dpa' rnams 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan dang gzhan du 'dong bas bskal brgyan tha dad pa'i tshul du gnas pa dang / 'di lta ste/ phyogs bcu'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho
113b1(phal chen): 'dus pas/ bskal pa mtha' yas brgyan shin tu mang por kun nas gnas pa dang / 'di lta ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa yongasu mya ngan las 'dra' bras 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mamo dag gi rgyan nu par
113b2(phal chen): 'gyur ba dang / 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas 'byung ba'i tshe 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho rnams rgyan gyis brgyan par kun nas gnas pa dang / 'di lta ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par 'phrul bas 'jig rten gyi khams
113b3(phal chen): rgya mtsho'i bskal pa mtha' yas pa yong su dag par gnas pa dang / de dag la sogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i bskal pa rgya mtsho mtha' yas pa'i rgyud kyi tshul rgya mtsho kun nas gnas pa'i tshul ni
113b4(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho rdul shin tu phra ba skad du shes par bya'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i bskal pa mtha' yas pa'i
113b5(phal chen): tshul rgya mtsho 'di nyid yongasu bstan pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byi na gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'itshig su bcad pa 'di dag smraso// zhing rnams rgya mtsho'i chos
113b6(phal chen): nyid 'di dag ltos// chos kyis byung ste ji ltar gnas pa ltar// de dag 'byung zhing 'jig par 'gyur bar yang // zhing rnams rgya mtsho thams cad rab tu snang // sems can nyon mongs mi bzang ldan
113b7(phal chen): pa dang / las dang nyon mongs ngan pas bsgribs pa'i rnams// de dag bsamal zhing gi rgya mtsho rnams// kun nas nyon mongs ldan par gyur pa yin// sems can rnam dag bsam pa ldan pa dang / 
113b8(phal chen): bsod nams brtan dang rnam dag spyod yul can// rnam dag yul la nyon mongs ldan gyur rnams// de dag mos pa sna tshogs spyod yul gyi// byang chub sems dpa' skye ba'i dus dag na// bskal
114a1(phal chen): bde ni rnam par dag par snang // sems can nyon mongs ldan par gyur pa yang // de'i chos shing bsam yas yangs pa yi// byang chub ba sam pa ji ltar bskyed pa dang / 
114a2(phal chen): de dag bsam pa ji ltar rnam 'phel bas// de bzhin bskal pa rgya mtsho mang po dag/ bsam gyis mi khyab zhing rgyan yongasu spyod // bye ba mang po mtha' yas mi zad pa'i// byang chub sems dpa' phyogs bcu kun rgyu
114a3(phal chen): yang // rgyan la rnam pa tha dad yod pa min// bskal pa tha dad tshul gyi bye phrag snang // rdul rnams re re sbub su dus kun tu// sangs rgyas zhing gi rdul dang mnyam pa yi// rgyal sras ji tshul 'dong ba de bzhin du/ 
114a4(phal chen): zhing rnams rgya mtsho tshul dag par gyur// gal te rgyal ba na/ mas ni skye 'gyur na// zhing rnams rgyan gyis shin tu brgyan pa ra 'gyur// bsam pa yongs dag de bzhin rgyas 'gyur te/ 
114a5(phal chen): 'di ni zhing rgyan phun sum tshogs pa'o// gal te rgyal brgya/ ngan 'das 'gyur na// de tshe de zhing rgyan rnams 'grib par 'gyur// sems can rnams kyang snod du rung ba min// zhing gi
114a6(phal chen): rgya mtsho de yang nyon mongs ldan// sangs rgyas rdzu 'phrul rnam 'phrul yangs pa dag/ bsam gyis mi khyab gang tshe ston pa na// de tshe zhing rnams rgya mtsho mang po dag/ kun kyang rgyan gyis rnam par
114a7(phal chen): brgyan par 'gyur// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho tha mi dad pa'i tshul ni/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du shes par bya ste/ de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom
114a8(phal chen): ldan 'das 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis gsungaso// gsung ngo // gsung bar 'gyur ro// de ni 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gcig tu
114b1(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra bsred kyi 'jig rten gyi khams tha mi dang pa dang / 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag tu/ sangs rgyas skye zhing 'byung ba tha mi dad pa dang / 'di lta ste/ 
114b2(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag gi snying po byang chub thams cad nas/ chos kyi dbyings kyis phyogs rgyas par 'gengs pa tha mi dad pa dang / 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag gi de bzhin ga bye
114b3(phal chen): pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor tha mi dad pa dang / 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag gi sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor chos kyi dbyings rgyas par 'gengs pa
114b4(phal chen): tha mi dad pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag tu sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sprul pa'i sprin dang / mtshan gyi 'khor lo tha mi dad pa dang / 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag
114b5(phal chen): tu sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor bskal pa mtha' yas par brjod cing rgyas par bya ba'i byin gyi rlabs tha mi dad pa dang / 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag
114b6(phal chen): tu chos kyi 'khor lo'i tshul tha mi da dang 'di sa ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag tu rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la'i'ajig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad yongs su 'du ba tha mi dad pa dang / 'di lta ste/ 
114b7(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho dag tu rdul 'byam klas pa thams cad la dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi yul rgya chen po ston cing rjod pa tha mi dad pa dag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de dag la sogs pa
114b8(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho tha mi dad pa'i tshul// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du shes par bya'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yang 'jig rten gyi kham
115a1(phal chen): rgya mtsho tha mi dad pa'i tshul rgya mtsho shin tu bstan pa 'di nying gsal bar bstan pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs/ 
115a2(phal chen): bcad pa 'di dag smraso// rdul gcig steng na zhing mang rgya mtsho ste// kun na rgyan mang rnam dag kun yod kyang // gnod pa med cing 'dre ba gang yang med// 'jug pa bsam gyis mi khyab 'di la ltos// rdul rnams
115a3(phal chen): kun la bsam yas sangs rgyas bzhugs// sems can kun gyi bsam pa yid bzhin du// zhing rnams rgya mtsho thams cad khyab byas kyang // de dag thabs la tha dad gang yang med// rdul rnams kun la shing
115a4(phal chen): dbang mtha' yas pa// sna tshogs rgyun phyung kun nas bres sgyu ngas te// phyogs rnams kun gyi zhing du mngon bkang yang // de drag za dang 'gyur ba nam yang med// rdul phran rgya mtsho rdul phran re re
115a5(phal chen): la// mi'i gtso bo 'khor rnams kun bskor cing // 'jig rte na kun tu bkang ste 'phags bzhugs kyang // gnod pa dag/ dang 'dre ba'i nyes pa med// rdul gaucig la ni mtha' yas 'od kyi
115a6(phal chen): sprin// phyogs bcu'i zhing rnams rgya mtsho kun bkang zhing // bde gshegs rnams kyi byang chub spyod bstan kyang // rgya mtsho'i zhing rnams tha dad gang yang med// rdul rnams kun la kha dog bsam mi kha
115a7(phal chen): sprul pa'i sprin gyis kun tu gang byas te// sangs rgyas sprul pas sems can rnams 'dul yang // 'byam klas phyogs na tha dad pa gang yang med// rdul rnams kun la rgya mtsho'i chos brjod de// de dag
115a8(phal chen): 'khor lo tshul bzhin 'khor mdzad cing // thabs dang mthu'i sgo mo sna tshogs kyis// thams cad brjod kyang de la tha dad med// rdul gcig la ni rgyal ba kun gyis gsung // 'gro ba snod du gyur la
115b1(phal chen): de dag brjod pas te// rgya mtsho'i zhing du bskal bar byin brlabs kyang // de dag gsung gi yan lag tha mi dang // zhing rnams rgya mtsho mtha' yas rgyan gyi rnams// thams cad rdul sbubs gcig tu rab tu
115b2(phal chen): 'jud// rgyal ba rnams kyi rdzu 'phrul mthu la ltos// las kyi dngos las de dag skyes pa min// rdul gcig la ni dus gsum rgyal ba dag/ ji ltar byung ba de dag thams cad snang // de dag gshegs dang
115b3(phal chen): byon pa gang yang med// 'gro ba kun na sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul// shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba las// 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho shin tu bstan pa'i phyogs
115b4(phal chen): gsal bar bya ba yang dag par bsgrubs pa zhes bya ba ste/ 'u bzhi pa'o// //  po brgang pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de la 'jig
115b5(phal chen): cher gyi khams rgya mcho ga zhi dang snying po me tog gi rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i nga bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam pa ra snang mdzad sngon byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa'i cha/ bas
115b6(phal chen): brgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba skad kyis yongasu dag par byas te/ bskal pa re re zhing yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi zhabs
115b7(phal chen): kyi drung du smon lam rgya mtsho 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis yongasu dag par byaso// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'jig can gyi khams rgya mcho ga zhi dang snying po ma tog gi rgyan
115b8(phal chen): gyis brgyan pa de ni rlung gi dkyil 'khor ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis shin tu bzung ba ste/ de la rlung gi dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi 'og ma ni/ gni kun nas rton pa zhes pa ste/ rin
116a1(phal chen): thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba 'bar bas brgyan pa'i gnyis rton to// de'i steng na rlung gi dkyil 'khor rin po che sna tshogs kyi rgyan 'byung ba zhes bya ba yod de/ nor bu'i
116a2(phal chen): rgyal po 'od rnam par dag pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi gzhis ston to// de'i steng na rlung gi dkyil 'khor rin po che'i mthu zhes bya ba yod de/ rin po che thams cad kyi dril bu'i gnyis rton to// de'i steng rlung
116a3(phal chen): gi dkyil 'khor 'od 'phro mnyam par rton pa zhes bya ba yod de/ nor bu'i rgyal po nyi ma snang ba'i rgyal mtshan gyi 'khor lo'i gzhis rton to// de'i steng na rlung gi dkyil 'khor rgya kun nas
116a4(phal chen): rnam par bres pa zhes bya ba yod de/ 'od zer gyi 'od kyi da dkyil 'khor gyi me tog gi gzhis rton to// de'i steng na rlung gi dkyil 'khor gzhi kun nas dri ma med cing yongasu
116a5(phal chen): dag pa zhes bya ba yod de/ me tog thams cad 'od 'phro ba 'i seng ge'i khri'i gzhis rton to// de'i steng na rlung gi dkyi la 'khor phyogasu sgra sgrog cing kun tu rgyu ba zhes bya ba yod de/ 
116a6(phal chen): mu tig dang man shel gyi rgyal mtshan sna tshogs kyi gzhis rton to// de'i steng na rlung gi dkyil 'khor rin po che thams cad 'dzin pa zhes bya ba yod de/ nor bu'i rgyal po'i shing dang me tog sna tshogs
116a7(phal chen): kyi glong gi gzhis rton to// de'i steng na rlung gi dkyil 'khor kun nas 'dzin pa'i shugs zhes bya ba yod de/ spos kyi nor bu thams cad kyi ri rab kyi sprin gyi gzhis rton to// de'i steng na rlung gi dkyil
116a8(phal chen): 'khor khyim kun tu rgyu ba zhes bya ba yod de/ rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog dang / spos kyi khang pa brtsegs pa'i sprin gyi gzhis rton to// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ rlung gi dkyil 'khor ri rab
116b1(phal chen): kyi rdul shin du phra ba snyed dag thams cad kyi steng pa ni rlung gi dkyil 'khor ga'i brjid bzang po dpal gyi snying po nas bya ste/ ne bukun nas snang ba'i rgyan dang ldan pa'i spos kyi su ma tsho gzhis nonas
116b2(phal chen): spos kyi chu rgyu mtsho nor bu kun nas snang ba'i gzhis brgyan pa'i snying po zhes bya ba de las pad+mo chen po spos kyi rgyal mtshan khyer ba'i 'od zer dang / ze ba sna tshogs shes bya ba mngon par 'byung ste/ pad+mo can
116b3(phal chen): bo da la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mcho gzhi dang snying po me tog ge rgyan gyi brgyan pa kun nas gru bzhir 'dug pa/ rnam par dag pa/ shin tu brtan pa/ rdo rje dang nor bu thams cad kyi khor yug gis bskor ba/ 
116b4(phal chen): rim gyis gzhol bar gnas pa/ shing gi rgyud rgya mtsho sa la rab tu gnas pa 'dug go// de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yang 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho ga ni dang snying po re
116b5(phal chen): tog gi rgyan pa 'di nyid kyi yon tan rgya mtsho yongasu dag pa 'i phyogs 'di zhing brjod pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i
116b6(phal chen): tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smraso// gzhi rgyan me tog 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgya mtsho de// rin chen kun gyi snying po kha dog sna chog sa te// rdul rnams kun dang mnyam pa'i sngan chang sangs
116b7(phal chen): rgyas kyi// drung du sngon tshe rgya mtshor sbyangs pas dri ma med// rgya chen snying rje'i sprin gyis khams rnams kun bkang zhing // zhing gi rdul dang mnyam pa'i lus kyang kun btang nas// sngon gyi
116b8(phal chen): bskal pa rgya mtshor spyod pa spyad pas na// 'jig rten rgya mtsho'i khams de yangs shing rnam par dag/ sangs rgyas rnam par snang bas smon lam che mdzad de// 'od snang gtang ba mkha'i
117a1(phal chen): dkyil na gnas pa ni// rlung gi phung pos btab kyang mi skyong mi g.yo ste/ nor bu kun rgyan sangs rgyas gzugs brnyan snying po'o// me tog mdzod bkye gtor b.rin chen yid
117a2(phal chen): 'ong bzhin// sngon gyi smon lam dbang gis mkha'i dbyings la gnas// rgya mtsho'i rgyan rnams thams cad sna tshogs brtan par gnas// phyogs dang phyogs mtshams kun tu 'od kyi sprin kyang gtong / 
117a3(phal chen): nor bu thams cad sgo nas byang chub sems dpa'i rnam// byung zhing 'od zer sprin 'bar phyogs rnams kun tu 'dong // 'od zer me tog tshon dang 'od zer 'khor lo'i tshogs// phyogs rnams ma lus kun gyi chos
117a4(phal chen): dbyings khyab par byed// rin chen kun gyis 'od zer sprin rnams bkye ba ni// phyogs dang phyogs mtshams kun gyi zhing rnams khyab par byed// sdug bsngal thams cad bcil zhing byang chub
117a5(phal chen): mchog la 'ged// 'jig rten rgya mtsho thams cad 'od 'gro rab tu 'bar// 'gro ba kun dang mnyam pa'i sprul pa sna tshogs rnams// rin chen kun dang spu rnams kun nas rgyal ba 'gyed/ 
117a6(phal chen): brgya byin dag dang tshangs pa'ang 'khor lo sgyu 'dra dang // 'gro ba kun gyi lus su lus rnams kun kyang gnas// sprul pas 'ong bkye chos kyi dbyings kyi tshad mnyam pa// 'od zer sgo nas sangs rgyas tham
117a7(phal chen): ca macan kyang sgrog/ 'gro ba ma lus kun gyi bsam pa chim byas nas// tshul rnams sna tshogs sgo nas sems can rnam par 'dul// 'jig rten rgya mtsho me tog snying po de nang na// rdul phran kun gyi khongasas
117a8(phal chen): chos dbyings thams cad kyi// rin chen 'od bkye sangs rgyas sprin rnams 'bar bar snang // rnam par snang mdzad rnam par 'phrul pa'i zhing la ltos// bskal pa rgya mtshor 'gro ba'i sdug bsngal bsal byas
117b1(phal chen): te/ smon lam yangs pa'i sprin ni chos kyi dbyings mnyam dang // bzang po'i spyod pa brnyes shing ye shes sa ldan pa'i// dgongs pa las ni rgyan mdzes de dag byung ba yin// shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo sangs/ 
117b2(phal chen): rgyas pal po che zhes bya ba las 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mchog ni dang snying po me tog gi rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i yon tan rgya mtsho yongasu dag pas snang ba zhes bya ba ste/ le'u lnga pa'o// 
117b3(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mcho ga ni dang snying po me tog gi rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i khor yug chen po ni nor bu'i rgyal po pad+mo nyi ma'i gzhi la brten pa ste/ nor bu'i rigs rgya mtsho spos kyi skad
117b4(phal chen): ngan thams cad las grub pa nor bu'i rgyal po rgyan gyi yul thams cad kyis lhun shin tu 'phags shing zil gyis gnon pa nor bu'i spos zhim po gzi brjid kyi 'khor lo rnam par snang ba'i snying
117b5(phal chen): can/ nor bu'i rgyal po rdo rje sra zhing mi shigs pa ltar shin tu mkhregs shing sra ba rin po che'i chu thams cad kun nas 'byung kha rin po che'i shing gi nags tshal gyi rgyan thams cad me tog
117b6(phal chen): shin tu rgyas pa/ spos kyi rtsi mchog bzang po thams cad kyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ spos kyi me tog dpal can shin tu bzang bas rnam par brgyan pa/ nor bu'i rgyal po 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi
117b7(phal chen): dbyibs lta bu'i dra bas kun nas bres pa ste/ de dag la sogs pargyan bzang po'i rnam pa 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba bsnyed kyis rab tu brgyan pa'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu
117b8(phal chen): bzang pos yang 'khor yug gi rgyan dang / yon tan yongasu dag pa 'di zhing bstan pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i mchig su bcang ba 'di dag smos/ 
118a1(phal chen): 'jig rten khams rnams rgya mtsho gang yod pa// mtha' dang dpung med sna tshogs rnam pa can// nor bu mang pos rnam dag mtha' yas mdog/ de dag sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul pas zung
118a2(phal chen): dri med khor yug rgyan gyis brgyan pa ni// nor bu mang po de bzhin spos mang dang // mu tig gsal ba'i tshogs la rab tu gnas// kha dog mtha' yas rin chen rnams kyis brtan// snying po nor bu'i sprin sna
118a3(phal chen): tshogs sra// 'dzam+bu chu klung 'od 'phro snying po'i tshigs// 'od 'phro dam pa phyogasu snang zhing 'tsher// khor yug dri ma med pa rnam par mdzes// nor bu rdo rjes 'dus byas shin tu sra shing brtan// mtshams
118a4(phal chen): rnams mi pang nor bu sna tshogs 'brul// mtshan ldan nor bu ni na chen rnam bkod pa// rgyan rnams kun gyis yongasu dag par snang // spos chu'i sgron gyis kha dog mtha' yas te// rin nen
118a5(phal chen): tsan dan me tog kun tu 'gram// pad+mo sna tshogs gos kyis du/ na nas yog/ rin chen rtsi mchog dri zhim rnams dang ldan// sna tshogs shing gi sprin gyis kun nas brgyan// nor bzang
118a6(phal chen): gyis kun nas gzi brjid 'bar// 'od zer sprin gyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor can// gos kyi mdzod kyis shin tu 'bar bar gnas// spos kyi 'od 'phro bdug pa'i gdugs 'chang ba'i// byang chub sems
118a7(phal chen): dpa' mang pos chos dbyings gang // sgra dbyangs mang po rgya mtsho thams cad 'byin// 'di ni rnam par snang mdzad chos 'khor lo// rin chen mdzes pa de dag thams cad dang // nor bu dag dang kun nas
118a8(phal chen): 'od 'phro'i shing // kun la rnam par snang mdzad sku gsal ba// gzugs brnyan tshul tu nang na yod pa snang // thams cad gzugasu sku rnams mtha' yas te// sangs rgyas sbrul mang kha dog mu med
118b1(phal chen): ba/ thams cad phyogs dang chos kyi dbyings bkang zhing // sems can mang po tshad med rnam par 'dul// thams cad rgyan las sgra dbyangs kun 'byung ste// rnam par snang mdzad smon lam 'khor lo
118b2(phal chen): yis// zhing rnams rgya mtsho yongs su dag byas pa// de kun de las rnam par 'phrul zhing grag/ shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba las/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i
118b3(phal chen): khor yug gi rgyan rgya mtsho shin tu bstan pa zhes bya ba ste/ le'u drug po'o// / kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de la khor yug chen po de'i nang ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i
118b4(phal chen): sa chen pa'i gzhi ni// nor bu mang po'i rgyan thams cad kyis brgyan pa/ rdo rje ltar shin tu 'khregs shing sral brtan pa/ rin po che'i rigs thams cad las grub pa/ rgya mtshos rnam
118b5(phal chen): par bye ba mi shigs pa'i snying po can/ mi mthong mi mnga' ba'i thang mnyam zhing rnam par dag pa/ nor bu rin po che tha mas cad kyi kha dog dang 'od thams cad kyis rab tu brgyan pa/ 
118b6(phal chen): sems can thams cad kyi lus kyi dbyibs lta bu'i nor bu'i gzugs sna tshogs kyis rab tu bsgrubs pa/ rin po che'i tshon thams cad kyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ rin po che yid du 'ong ba'i pad+ma thams
118b7(phal chen): cad kyis gzhi bas pa/ dmigs pa thams cad du sna tshogasu gyur pa'i sprin gyis kun nas yog pa/ nor bu'i rgyal po spos kyi mdzod thams cad kyis gzhi mnyam par bdal ba/ nor bu'i rgyal po
118b8(phal chen): dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhing gi rgyan gyi sprin gyi drang rnam par bris pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi spyod yul gyi 'od dang / nor bu'i dra ba mig 'phrul lnga bu rnam par phye ba ste/ 
119a1(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de dag la sogs pa sa'i dkyil 'khor de'i rgyun shin tu bstan pa ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed do// de nas byang chub sems dpa'

119a3(phal chen): dkyil 'khor gzhi ni rnam dag mnyam// 'khor lo'i dra bas bsgrubs pas mi shigs sra// rin chen sna tshogs mnyam pa'i gzhir gnas shing // rin chen sna tshogs kun gyis kun tu gang // yid 'ongs ni
119a4(phal chen): rdo rje gser gyi gzhi// rin chen chub ri bo'i 'khor los bsgrubs// pad+mo dkyil 'khor gzhi yin me tog sa// tsan dan phye ma rin chen kun tu bkram// 'od zer sna tshogs rin chen me tog
119a5(phal chen): rnams// 'od 'phro 'gyeng bas phyogs su sprin kyang 'bar/ sangs rgyas 'od snang nor bu rnam par bkram// sa ku/ na me tog yid du 'ong bas yog/ thams cad sprin ni phyogs na
119a6(phal chen): sdug lding bas// mi zad yangs pa kun nas khebs par 'dug/ zhing rnams thams cad phyogs rnams kun bkang zhing // sangs rgyas chos ni snyan par rab tu sgrog/ rin chen nang snang sangs rgyas
119a7(phal chen): smon lam kun// shin tu dus ring rtag tu kun tu ston// sngan chad spyod pa ji 'dra spyod pa dag/ kun kyang nor bu'i 'bru las gsal bar snang // de'i rgya mtsho nor bu sna tshogs gting // de'i nang na sangs rgyas
119a8(phal chen): spyod yul snang // sangs rgyas spyod yul de dag zhing gi rnams// rgya mtsho kun gyi rdul phran re rar snang // me tog snying po tshon gyi 'khor los bsgrubs// der ni byang chub sems dpa' rtag 'dong zhig/ 
119b1(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam kun kyang sgeg/ snying po byang chub 'khor du rnam 'phrulo// rin chen 'od zer 'od dang ldan pa dag/ sa'i nor bu rgyan las rab tu 'byung // sangs rgyas chos nyid 'di yang rtag tu
119b2(phal chen): ston// chos dbyings na mkha' lta bu kun tu 'gengs// sangs rgyas kun yul ye shes rgya chen dang // kun tu bzang po'i smon lam sus shes pa// de dag phyogs rnams rgya mtsho kun tu yang // zhing
119b3(phal chen): rnams rgya mtsho dbyings kyi 'phrul la 'jug/ shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo// sangs rgyas pal po che zhes bya ba las/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i sa'i gzhi'i rgyun shin tu bstan pa zhes bya ba ste/ 
119b4(phal chen): le'u bdun pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag/ de la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i gzhi sa'i dkyil 'a khor de la spos chu'i rgya mtsho sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i
119b5(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yod de// de dag kun kyang gzhi rin po n+da thams cad kyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa'o// nor bu'i rgyal po dang spros thams cad kyis klung rab tu bsgrubs po'o// nor bu'i
119b6(phal chen): rgyal po bzang zhing yid du 'ong ba'i 'od rnam par snang ba'i dra bas kun nas bres pa'o// rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog dang mchog tu snang ba'i spos kyi chus yongasu rgyas pa'o// rin po che thams
119b7(phal chen): cad kyi me tog sna tshogs klong du khyil po'o// tsan dan gyi bye ma dang 'dres pa'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsung gi dkyil 'khor dang / smon lam rgya mtsho'i sgra 'byin pa'o// rin po che thams
119b8(phal chen): cad kyi 'od zer gyi dkyil 'khor gyi sprin rnam par snang ba'o// byang chub sems dpa'i lus kyi sprin me tog sna tshogs kyi kha dog lta bur rab tu 'gyeng ba'o// kha dog dang dbyibs mtha' yas pa'i
120a1(phal chen): gdugs kyis khebs par rnam par 'phrul pas brgyan pa'o// dmigs pa thams cad la 'jig rten gyi khams mang po rgya chen po thams cad snang ba'o// phyogs kun nas rin po
120a2(phal chen): che'i them skas kyi phreng ba bcur rab tu bkye ba'o// mu tig rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog lta bu'i mu khyud kyis kun nas bskor ba'o// rin po che shel gyi rgyal mtshan bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du mang ba bcus
120a3(phal chen): kun nas brgyan pa'o// 'di lta ste/ nor bu dang me tog gi khang pa brtsegs pa chu klung gang+gA'iri klung gi bye ma snyed kha deg mtha' yas pa bcus kun nas bskor ba'o// 'di lta ste/ nor bu thams cad kyi pad+mo yid du 'ong
120a4(phal chen): ba'i grong khyer bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag bcus kun nas bskor ba'o// 'di lta ste/ nor bu rdo rje shin tu sra ba gling bzhi'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba sbed kyis rab tu bsgrubs pa'o// 
120a5(phal chen): rin po che thams cad kyi me tog pun da ri ka dang / spos kyi chu yod/ su rgyas pas kun nas bskor ba'o// 'di lta ste rin po che/ 'i shing gi phreng ba rin po che 'bar zhing kun nas 'phang ba'i nor bu'i
120a6(phal chen): dra ba can gling bzhi'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis kun nas bskor ba'o// tsan dan dang spros dang / nor bu mang po sgra thams cad dang sangs rgyas kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi phyag gis rnam
120a7(phal chen): par snang bar bas pa/ chu klung gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed kyis 'gram shin tu brgyan po'o// 'di lta ste/ rin po che dang / gos dang / rgyal mtshan dang / dril bu mang po thams cad kyi sgra 'byung bas rgyan
120a8(phal chen): shin tu rgyas pa'o// rin po che yid du 'ong ba'i nor bu thams cad kyi rab bya ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pas kun nas bskor ba'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos yang spos chu rgya

120b2(phal chen): shus brgyan pa rnam brjod de// gzhi rnams rin chen gos kyis kun bting ba// mi shogs rdo rje lta bu sra zhing mdzes// spos dang nor bu'i rgyal po mang po dang // nyi ma'i nor bu 'od 'phro stug sprin dang //

123b6(phal chen): cad kyang // rin chen rgyan can 'od zer gnas pa ste// sdug cing bskul pa'i sprin gyis kun nas yog/ rin chen thams cad 'od kyang rnam par 'bar// mu tog nor bu'i sprin mang zad mi shes/

123b8(phal chen): mi khyab ste// nor bu'i rgyal po thams cad snyan par sgrog/ rnam par snang mdzad sngon gyi spyod pa rnams// rin chen rnams la rtag par snang zhing grag/ sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad dri meda'ang // rgyan
124a1(phal chen): thams cad nang na rnam par snang // 'khor rnams gzugs brnyan mtshan nyid 'chang ba dang // sprul pa rnams kyis zhing gi rgya mtsho gang // sangs rgyas sprul pa rnams ni sgyu ma 'a
124a2(phal chen): de dag la ni byon pa gang yang med// sangs rgyas yul rnams byin gyis brlabs pa yi// zhing rnams kun na sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul// zhing rnams 'byam klas par ni rnam 'phrul zhing / 
124a3(phal chen): steng zhing du de dag kun rgyu ba// de dag nor bu kun la rab tu snang // de ltar zhing gi rgya mtsho rnam par sbyangs// sprul pa rnams ni mig yor 'dra ba ste// thams cad dag na chos nyid 'di yang snang // 'di ni
124a4(phal chen): rnam par snang mdzad spyod yul te// smon lam rnam par 'phrul las byung ba'o// bzang po'i spyod pas gang rnams byung gyur pa'i// byang chub sems dpa' shes mchog rgya mtsho can// de dag rdul
124a5(phal chen): phran kun la rang rang gis// rang gi zhing rnams rgya mtsho dag pa/ 'byed// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi zham rang du// bskal pa bye ba rgya chen bsam yas su// de dag spyong yul tham/ 
124a6(phal chen): cad mthong bas na// skad cig sems la de dag thams cad ston// zhing rnams mnyam med 'byung ba med pa ste// de dag mtha' 'dra mnyam zhing mtshan nyid med// smon lam stobs kyis kun tu gnas
124a7(phal chen): ba ste// sems can rnams la phan phyir rab tu sbyangs// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de la 'jig rten gyi khams rnam par dgod pa shin tu bstan pa gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'jig rten gyi khams/
